            BuildingBlock {
                name: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                width: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                height: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                area: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for BuildingBlock {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> BuildingBlock {
            BuildingBlock {
                name: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.name),
                width: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.width),
                height: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.height),
                num_pins: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.num_pins),
                pins: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.pins),
                area: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.area),
            }
        }
    }
    impl BuildingBlock {
        pub fn new(name: String, width: float, height: float, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            let area = width * height;
            let pins = ListMap::default();
            Self {
                name,
                width,
                height,
                num_pins,
                pins,
                area,
            }
        }
    }
    pub struct IOput {
        cell: BuildingBlock,
        is_input: bool,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for IOput {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field2_finish(
                f,
                "IOput",
                "cell",
                &self.cell,
                "is_input",
                &&self.is_input,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for IOput {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> IOput {
            IOput {
                cell: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                is_input: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for IOput {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> IOput {
            IOput {
                cell: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.cell),
                is_input: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.is_input),
            }
        }
    }
    impl IOput {
        pub fn new(is_input: bool) -> Self {
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(String::new(), 0.0, 0.0, 1);
            let mut input = Self { cell: cell, is_input };
            input.cell.pins.push(String::new(), Pin::new(String::new(), 0.0, 0.0));
            input
        }
    }
    pub struct Gate {
        pub cell: BuildingBlock,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Gate {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field1_finish(
                f,
                "Gate",
                "cell",
                &&self.cell,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Gate {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Gate {
            Gate {
                cell: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.cell),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Gate {
        pub fn new(name: String, width: float, height: float, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(name, width, height, num_pins);
            Self { cell }
        }
    }
    pub struct FlipFlop {
        pub cell: BuildingBlock,
        pub bits: uint,
        pub qpin_delay: float,
        pub power: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for FlipFlop {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "FlipFlop",
                "cell",
                &self.cell,
                "bits",
                &self.bits,
                "qpin_delay",
                &self.qpin_delay,
                "power",
                &&self.power,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for FlipFlop {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> FlipFlop {
            FlipFlop {
                cell: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.cell),
                bits: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.bits),
                qpin_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.qpin_delay),
                power: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.power),
            }
        }
    }
    impl FlipFlop {
        pub fn new(
            bits: uint,
            name: String,
            width: float,
            height: float,
            num_pins: uint,
        ) -> Self {
            let power = 0.0;
            let qpin_delay = 0.0;
            let cell = BuildingBlock::new(name, width, height, num_pins);
            Self {
                cell: cell,
                bits,
                qpin_delay,
                power,
            }
        }
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<Reference<Pin>> {
            self.cell
                .pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow_mut().name.to_lowercase().starts_with("d"))
                .map(|pin| clone_ref(pin))
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn evaluate_power_area_ratio(&self, mbffg: &MBFFG) -> float {
            (mbffg.power_weight() * self.power + mbffg.area_weight() * self.cell.area)
                / self.bits.float()
        }
        pub fn evaluate_power_area_score(&self, mbffg: &MBFFG) -> float {
            mbffg.power_weight() * self.power + mbffg.area_weight() * self.cell.area
        }
        pub fn name(&self) -> &String {
            &self.cell.name
        }
        pub fn bits(&self) -> uint {
            self.bits
        }
        pub fn width(&self) -> float {
            self.cell.width
        }
        pub fn height(&self) -> float {
            self.cell.height
        }
        /// returns the (width, height) of the flip-flop
        pub fn size(&self) -> Vector2 {
            (self.width(), self.height())
        }
        /// Calculates the grid coverage of the flip-flop within a given placement row.
        /// Returns a tuple containing the number of grid cells covered in the x and y directions.
        pub fn grid_coverage(&self, placement_row: &PlacementRows) -> (uint, uint) {
            let (width, height) = (placement_row.width, placement_row.height);
            let (w, h) = (self.width(), self.height());
            let (x, y) = ((h / height).ceil(), (w / width).ceil());
            (x.uint(), y.uint())
        }
    }
    pub enum InstType {
        FlipFlop(FlipFlop),
        Gate(Gate),
        IOput(IOput),
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for InstType {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "FlipFlop",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
                InstType::Gate(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "Gate",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
                InstType::IOput(__self_0) => {
                    ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_tuple_field1_finish(
                        f,
                        "IOput",
                        &__self_0,
                    )
                }
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for InstType {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> InstType {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(__self_0) => {
                    InstType::FlipFlop(::core::clone::Clone::clone(__self_0))
                }
                InstType::Gate(__self_0) => {
                    InstType::Gate(::core::clone::Clone::clone(__self_0))
                }
                InstType::IOput(__self_0) => {
                    InstType::IOput(::core::clone::Clone::clone(__self_0))
                }
            }
        }
    }
    pub trait InstTrait {
        fn property(&mut self) -> &mut BuildingBlock;
        fn property_ref(&self) -> &BuildingBlock;
        fn ff(&mut self) -> &mut FlipFlop;
        fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.ff_ref().qpin_delay
        }
        fn is_ff(&self) -> bool;
        fn ff_ref(&self) -> &FlipFlop;
        fn pins(&self) -> &ListMap<String, Pin> {
            &self.property_ref().pins
        }
    }
    impl InstTrait for InstType {
        fn property(&mut self) -> &mut BuildingBlock {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => &mut flip_flop.cell,
                InstType::Gate(gate) => &mut gate.cell,
                InstType::IOput(ioput) => &mut ioput.cell,
            }
        }
        fn property_ref(&self) -> &BuildingBlock {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => &flip_flop.cell,
                InstType::Gate(gate) => &gate.cell,
                InstType::IOput(ioput) => &ioput.cell,
            }
        }
        fn ff(&mut self) -> &mut FlipFlop {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => flip_flop,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("{0} is Not a flip-flop", self.property().name),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        fn ff_ref(&self) -> &FlipFlop {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(flip_flop) => flip_flop,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Not a flip-flop"));
                }
            }
        }
        fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            match self {
                InstType::FlipFlop(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
    }
    pub struct PrevFFRecord {
        pub ff_q: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub ff_d: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub travel_dist: float,
        displacement_delay: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for PrevFFRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> PrevFFRecord {
            PrevFFRecord {
                ff_q: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_q),
                ff_d: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_d),
                travel_dist: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.travel_dist),
                displacement_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.displacement_delay),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Hash for PrevFFRecord {
        fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            self.id().hash(state);
        }
    }
    impl PartialEq for PrevFFRecord {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            self.id() == other.id()
        }
    }
    impl Eq for PrevFFRecord {}
    impl PrevFFRecord {
        pub fn new(displacement_delay: float) -> Self {
            Self {
                ff_q: None,
                ff_d: None,
                travel_dist: 0.0,
                displacement_delay,
            }
        }
        pub fn id(&self) -> (usize, usize) {
            if let Some((ff_q, ff_d)) = &self.ff_q {
                (ff_q.get_id(), ff_d.get_id())
            } else {
                (0, 0)
            }
        }
        pub fn set_ff_q(mut self, ff_q: (SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)) -> Self {
            self.ff_q = Some(ff_q);
            self
        }
        pub fn set_travel_dist(mut self, travel_dist: float) -> Self {
            self.travel_dist = travel_dist;
            self
        }
        pub fn has_ff_q(&self) -> bool {
            self.ff_q.is_some()
        }
        pub fn has_ff_d(&self) -> bool {
            self.ff_d.is_some()
        }
        pub fn ff_q_dist(&self) -> float {
            if let Some((ff_q, con)) = &self.ff_q {
                ff_q.get_mapped_pin().distance(&con.get_mapped_pin())
            } else {
                0.0
            }
        }
        pub fn ff_d_dist(&self) -> float {
            if let Some((ff_d, con)) = &self.ff_d {
                ff_d.get_mapped_pin().distance(&con.get_mapped_pin())
            } else {
                0.0
            }
        }
        pub fn ff_q_src(&self) -> Option<&SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.ff_q.as_ref().map(|(ff_q, _)| ff_q)
        }
        pub fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.ff_q_src().map_or(0.0, |x| x.get_mapped_pin().qpin_delay())
        }
        pub fn ff_q_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.displacement_delay * self.ff_q_dist()
        }
        pub fn ff_d_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.displacement_delay * self.ff_d_dist()
        }
        pub fn travel_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.displacement_delay * self.travel_dist
        }
        pub fn calculate_total_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.qpin_delay() + self.ff_q_delay() + self.ff_d_delay()
                + self.travel_delay()
        }
        /// timing delay without capture ff's D-pin wirelength
        pub fn calculate_total_delay_wo_capture(&self) -> float {
            let sink_wl = if self.has_ff_d() { self.ff_q_delay() } else { 0.0 };
            self.qpin_delay() + sink_wl + self.travel_delay()
        }
        pub fn dpin(&self) -> &SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.ff_d
                .as_ref()
                .or_else(|| self.ff_q.as_ref())
                .map(|x| &x.1)
                .expect("dpin is not found in PrevFFRecord")
        }
        pub fn calculate_neg_slack(&self) -> float {
            let ff_d = self.dpin();
            let slack = ff_d.get_slack() + ff_d.get_origin_delay()
                - self.calculate_total_delay();
            (-slack).max(0.0)
        }
        pub fn ff_q(&self) -> &(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.ff_q.as_ref().unwrap()
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Debug for PrevFFRecord {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            let ff_str = |x: &Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>| {
                x.as_ref()
                    .map(|(ff_q_src, ff_q)| {
                        ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!(
                                    "{0} -> {1}",
                                    ff_q_src.borrow().full_name().clone(),
                                    ff_q.borrow().full_name().clone(),
                                ),
                            );
                            res
                        })
                    })
                    .or_else(|| Some("".into()))
                    .unwrap()
            };
            f.debug_struct("PrevFFRecord")
                .field("ff_q", &ff_str(&self.ff_q))
                .field("ff_q_dist", &round(self.ff_q_dist(), 2))
                .field("ff_d", &ff_str(&self.ff_d))
                .field("ff_d_dist", &round(self.ff_d_dist(), 2))
                .field("travel_delay", &self.travel_dist)
                .field(
                    "sum_dist",
                    &round(self.ff_q_dist() + self.ff_d_dist() + self.travel_dist, 2),
                )
                .field("displacement_delay", &self.displacement_delay)
                .field("total_delay", &round(self.calculate_total_delay(), 2))
                .finish()
        }
    }
    pub struct PrevFFRecorder {
        map: Dict<QPinId, Dict<PinId, PrevFFRecord>>,
        queue: PriorityQueue<(PinId, PinId), OrderedFloat<float>>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for PrevFFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> PrevFFRecorder {
            PrevFFRecorder {
                map: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                queue: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for PrevFFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> PrevFFRecorder {
            PrevFFRecorder {
                map: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.map),
                queue: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.queue),
            }
        }
    }
    impl PrevFFRecorder {
        pub fn from(records: &Set<PrevFFRecord>) -> Self {
            let mut map = Dict::new();
            let mut queue = PriorityQueue::with_capacity_and_default_hasher(
                records.len(),
            );
            for record in records {
                let id = record.id();
                map.entry(id.0)
                    .or_insert_with(Dict::new)
                    .entry(id.1)
                    .or_insert_with(|| record.clone());
                queue.push(id, record.calculate_total_delay_wo_capture().into());
            }
            Self { map, queue }
        }
        pub fn update_delay(&mut self, id: QPinId) {
            for (_, record) in &self.map[&id] {
                self.queue
                    .change_priority(
                        &record.id(),
                        record.calculate_total_delay_wo_capture().into(),
                    );
            }
        }
        pub fn refresh(&mut self) {
            for records in self.map.values() {
                for record in records.values() {
                    let priority = record.calculate_total_delay_wo_capture().into();
                    self.queue.change_priority(&record.id(), priority);
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn peek(&self) -> Option<&PrevFFRecord> {
            self.queue.peek().map(|(id, _)| &self.map[&id.0][&id.1])
        }
        pub fn get_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.peek().map_or(0.0, |record| record.calculate_total_delay())
        }
        pub fn count(&self) -> usize {
            self.queue.len()
        }
    }
    pub struct NextFFRecorder {
        list: Set<DPinId>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for NextFFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> NextFFRecorder {
            NextFFRecorder {
                list: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for NextFFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> NextFFRecorder {
            NextFFRecorder {
                list: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.list),
            }
        }
    }
    impl NextFFRecorder {
        pub fn add(&mut self, pin: DPinId) {
            self.list.insert(pin);
        }
        pub fn get(&self) -> &Set<DPinId> {
            &self.list
        }
        pub fn size(&self) -> usize {
            self.list.len()
        }
    }
    pub struct FFRecorder {
        map: Dict<DPinId, (PrevFFRecorder, NextFFRecorder, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for FFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> FFRecorder {
            FFRecorder {
                map: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for FFRecorder {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> FFRecorder {
            FFRecorder {
                map: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.map),
            }
        }
    }
    impl FFRecorder {
        pub fn new(cache: &Dict<SharedPhysicalPin, Set<PrevFFRecord>>) -> Self {
            let mut map: Dict<
                DPinId,
                (PrevFFRecorder, NextFFRecorder, SharedPhysicalPin),
            > = cache
                .iter()
                .map(|(pin, records)| {
                    let prev_recorder = PrevFFRecorder::from(records);
                    (
                        pin.get_id(),
                        (prev_recorder, NextFFRecorder::default(), pin.clone()),
                    )
                })
                .collect();
            for (pin, records) in cache {
                for record in records.iter().filter(|x| x.has_ff_q()) {
                    map.get_mut(&record.ff_q_src().unwrap().corresponding_pin().get_id())
                        .unwrap()
                        .1
                        .add(pin.get_id());
                }
            }
            Self { map }
        }
        pub fn get_next_ffs(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> &Set<DPinId> {
            self.map[&pin.get_id()].1.get()
        }
        pub fn get_next_ffs_count(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> usize {
            self.get_next_ffs(pin).len()
        }
        pub fn get_delay(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            self.map[&pin.get_id()].0.get_delay()
        }
        pub fn update_delay(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            let downstream = self.get_next_ffs(pin).iter().cloned().collect_vec();
            let q_id = pin.corresponding_pin().get_id();
            for x in downstream {
                self.map.get_mut(&x).unwrap().0.update_delay(q_id);
            }
        }
        /// Peek for largest delay record..
        pub fn peek(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> Option<&PrevFFRecord> {
            self.map.get(&pin.get_id()).unwrap().0.peek()
        }
        pub fn pin_neg_slack(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            self.peek(pin).map(|x| x.calculate_neg_slack()).unwrap_or(0.0)
        }
        pub fn effected_pin_records<'a>(
            &'a self,
            pin: &'a SharedPhysicalPin,
        ) -> impl Iterator<Item = &'a PrevFFRecord> {
            if !pin.is_d_pin() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: pin.is_d_pin()")
            }
            self.get_next_ffs(pin)
                .iter()
                .filter_map(|dpin_id| {
                    let record = &self.map[dpin_id].0.peek();
                    if let Some(record) = record {
                        if let Some(ff_q_src) = record.ff_q_src() {
                            if ff_q_src.get_id() == pin.corresponding_pin().get_id() {
                                Some(*record)
                            } else {
                                None
                            }
                        } else {
                            None
                        }
                    } else {
                        None
                    }
                })
        }
        pub fn effected_num(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> usize {
            self.effected_pin_records(pin).count()
        }
        pub fn effected_neg_slack(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            self.pin_neg_slack(pin)
                + self
                    .effected_pin_records(pin)
                    .map(|x| x.calculate_neg_slack())
                    .sum::<float>()
        }
        pub fn inst_effected_neg_slack(&self, inst: &SharedInst) -> float {
            inst.dpins()
                .iter()
                .map(|pin| self.effected_neg_slack(&pin.ff_origin_pin()))
                .sum()
        }
        pub fn update_delay_all(&mut self) {
            self.map
                .values_mut()
                .for_each(|(prev, _, _)| {
                    prev.refresh();
                });
        }
    }
    pub struct TimingRecord {
        pub ff_q: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub ff_d: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
        pub travel_dist: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for TimingRecord {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> TimingRecord {
            TimingRecord {
                ff_q: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_q),
                ff_d: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ff_d),
                travel_dist: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.travel_dist),
            }
        }
    }
    impl TimingRecord {
        pub fn new(
            ff_q: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
            ff_d: Option<(SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin)>,
            travel_dist: float,
        ) -> Self {
            Self { ff_q, ff_d, travel_dist }
        }
        fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.ff_q.as_ref().map_or(0.0, |(ff_q, _)| ff_q.borrow().qpin_delay())
        }
        fn ff_q_dist(&self) -> float {
            if let Some((ff_q, con)) = &self.ff_q { ff_q.distance(&con) } else { 0.0 }
        }
        fn ff_d_dist(&self) -> float {
            if let Some((ff_d, con)) = &self.ff_d { ff_d.distance(&con) } else { 0.0 }
        }
        pub fn total(&self, displacement_delay: float) -> float {
            self.qpin_delay()
                + (self.ff_q_dist() + self.ff_d_dist() + self.travel_dist)
                    * displacement_delay
        }
    }
    impl fmt::Debug for TimingRecord {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("TimingRecord")
                .field(
                    "ff_q",
                    &self
                        .ff_q
                        .as_ref()
                        .map(|(ff_q_src, ff_q)| {
                            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!(
                                        "{0} -> {1}",
                                        ff_q_src.full_name(),
                                        ff_q.full_name(),
                                    ),
                                );
                                res
                            })
                        }),
                )
                .field("ff_q_dist", &round(self.ff_q_dist(), 2))
                .field("ff_d_dist", &round(self.ff_d_dist(), 2))
                .field("travel_dist", &round(self.travel_dist, 2))
                .field(
                    "total dist",
                    &(round(self.ff_q_dist() + self.ff_d_dist() + self.travel_dist, 2)),
                )
                .finish()
        }
    }
    static mut PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER: usize = 0;
    pub struct PhysicalPin {
        pub net_name: String,
        pub inst: WeakInst,
        pub pin: WeakReference<Pin>,
        pub pin_name: String,
        slack: Option<float>,
        origin_pin: Option<WeakPhysicalPin>,
        mapped_pin: Option<WeakPhysicalPin>,
        origin_delay: Option<float>,
        pub merged: bool,
        #[hash]
        pub id: usize,
        x: float,
        y: float,
        pub corresponding_pin: Option<SharedPhysicalPin>,
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for PhysicalPin {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            true && self.id == other.id
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for PhysicalPin {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for PhysicalPin {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            self.id.hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct SharedPhysicalPin(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>);
    impl SharedPhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(value: PhysicalPin) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<PhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<PhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            WeakPhysicalPin(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        pub fn get_net_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.net_name)
        }
        pub fn get_net_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.net_name)
        }
        pub fn set_net_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().net_name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_inst(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakInst> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.inst)
        }
        pub fn get_inst_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakInst> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.inst)
        }
        pub fn set_inst(&self, value: WeakInst) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().inst = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_pin(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakReference<Pin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pin)
        }
        pub fn get_pin_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakReference<Pin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pin)
        }
        pub fn set_pin(&self, value: WeakReference<Pin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pin = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_pin_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pin_name)
        }
        pub fn get_pin_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pin_name)
        }
        pub fn set_pin_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pin_name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_merged(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().merged
        }
        pub fn get_merged_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.merged)
        }
        pub fn set_merged(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().merged = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_id(&self) -> usize {
            self.borrow().id
        }
        pub fn get_id_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<usize> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.id)
        }
        pub fn set_id(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().id = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_corresponding_pin(
            &self,
        ) -> std::cell::Ref<Option<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.corresponding_pin)
        }
        pub fn get_corresponding_pin_mut(
            &self,
        ) -> std::cell::RefMut<Option<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(
                self.borrow_mut(),
                |inner| &mut inner.corresponding_pin,
            )
        }
        pub fn set_corresponding_pin(&self, value: Option<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().corresponding_pin = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedPhysicalPin").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>> for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<PhysicalPin> for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: PhysicalPin) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedPhysicalPin> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedPhysicalPin) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            *self.0.borrow() == *other.0.borrow()
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for SharedPhysicalPin {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for SharedPhysicalPin {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            (&*self.0 as *const _ as usize).hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakPhysicalPin(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>);
    impl WeakPhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedPhysicalPin::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        pub fn set_net_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().net_name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_inst(&self, value: WeakInst) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().inst = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_pin(&self, value: WeakReference<Pin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pin = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_pin_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pin_name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_merged(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().merged
        }
        pub fn set_merged(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().merged = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_id(&self) -> usize {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().id
        }
        pub fn set_id(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().id = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_corresponding_pin(&self, value: Option<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().corresponding_pin = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakPhysicalPin")
                .field("is_expired", &self.is_expired())
                .finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>> for WeakPhysicalPin {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakPhysicalPin> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<PhysicalPin>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakPhysicalPin) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl PhysicalPin {
        pub fn new(inst: &SharedInst, pin: &Reference<Pin>) -> Self {
            let inst = inst.downgrade();
            let (x, y) = pin.borrow().pos();
            let pin = clone_weak_ref(pin);
            let pin_name = pin.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().name.clone();
            Self {
                net_name: String::new(),
                inst,
                pin,
                pin_name,
                slack: None,
                origin_pin: None,
                mapped_pin: None,
                origin_delay: None,
                merged: false,
                id: unsafe {
                    PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER += 1;
                    PHYSICAL_PIN_COUNTER
                },
                x,
                y,
                corresponding_pin: None,
            }
        }
        pub fn inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().clone()
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            let posx = self.inst().get_x() + self.x;
            let posy = self.inst().get_y() + self.y;
            (posx, posy)
        }
        pub fn start_pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            let ori_pos = self.get_origin_pin().inst().start_pos();
            (ori_pos.0 + self.x, ori_pos.1 + self.y)
        }
        pub fn inst_name(&self) -> String {
            self.inst().get_name().clone()
        }
        pub fn full_name(&self) -> String {
            if self.pin_name.is_empty() {
                return self.inst().borrow().name.clone();
            } else {
                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                        format_args!("{0}/{1}", self.inst_name(), self.pin_name),
                    );
                    res
                })
            }
        }
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_ff()
        }
        pub fn is_d_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with('d') || self.pin_name.starts_with('D'))
        }
        pub fn is_q_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with('q') || self.pin_name.starts_with('Q'))
        }
        pub fn is_clk_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_ff()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("clk") || self.pin_name.starts_with("CLK"))
        }
        pub fn is_gate(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_gt()
        }
        pub fn is_gate_in(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_gt()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("in") || self.pin_name.starts_with("IN"))
        }
        pub fn is_gate_out(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_gt()
                && (self.pin_name.starts_with("out") || self.pin_name.starts_with("OUT"))
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().is_io()
        }
        pub fn set_walked(&self, walked: bool) {
            self.inst().set_walked(walked);
        }
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, highlighted: bool) {
            self.inst().set_highlighted(highlighted);
        }
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.inst().get_gid()
        }
        pub fn is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.inst().get_is_origin()
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            norm1(self.pos(), other.pos())
        }
        pub fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.inst.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().lib.borrow().ff_ref().qpin_delay
        }
        pub fn record_origin_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            if !self.origin_pin.is_none() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "{1}{0} already has an origin pin{2}",
                            self.full_name(),
                            color_red,
                            color_reset,
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.origin_pin = Some(pin.downgrade());
        }
        pub fn change_origin_pin(&mut self, pin: WeakPhysicalPin) {
            self.origin_pin = Some(pin);
        }
        pub fn get_origin_pin(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            if self.origin_pin.as_ref().unwrap().get_id() == self.id {
                self.origin_pin.as_ref().unwrap().clone()
            } else {
                self.origin_pin.as_ref().map(|x| x.get_origin_pin()).unwrap()
            }
        }
        pub fn ff_origin_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "{1}{0} is not a flip-flop{2}",
                            self.full_name(),
                            color_red,
                            color_reset,
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.get_origin_pin().upgrade().unwrap()
        }
        pub fn previous_pin(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            self.origin_pin.as_ref().cloned().unwrap()
        }
        pub fn get_origin_id(&self) -> usize {
            self.get_origin_pin().get_id()
        }
        pub fn record_mapped_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.mapped_pin = Some(pin.downgrade());
        }
        pub fn get_mapped_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            if self.mapped_pin.as_ref().unwrap().get_id() == self.id {
                self.mapped_pin.as_ref().unwrap().upgrade().unwrap()
            } else {
                self.mapped_pin.as_ref().map(|x| x.get_mapped_pin()).unwrap()
            }
        }
        fn assert_is_d_pin(&self) {
            if !self.is_d_pin() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "{1}{0} is not a D pin{2}",
                            self.full_name(),
                            color_red,
                            color_reset,
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn get_origin_delay(&mut self) -> float {
            self.assert_is_d_pin();
            if self.is_origin() {
                return self.origin_delay.unwrap();
            } else {
                self.origin_pin.as_ref().unwrap().get_origin_delay()
            }
        }
        pub fn set_origin_delay(&mut self, value: float) {
            self.assert_is_d_pin();
            if !self.origin_delay.is_none() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "Origin delay already set for {0}",
                            self.full_name(),
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.origin_delay = Some(value);
        }
        pub fn get_slack(&mut self) -> float {
            self.assert_is_d_pin();
            if self.is_origin() {
                return self.slack.unwrap();
            } else {
                self.origin_pin.as_ref().unwrap().get_slack()
            }
        }
        pub fn set_slack(&mut self, value: float) {
            self.assert_is_d_pin();
            if !self.slack.is_none() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Slack already set for {0}", self.full_name()),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.slack = Some(value);
        }
        pub fn get_qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.inst().get_lib().borrow().qpin_delay()
        }
        pub fn corresponding_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.corresponding_pin.as_ref().cloned().unwrap()
        }
    }
    impl SharedPhysicalPin {
        pub fn inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.0.borrow().inst()
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().pos()
        }
        pub fn start_pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().start_pos()
        }
        pub fn inst_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().inst_name()
        }
        pub fn full_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().full_name()
        }
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_ff()
        }
        pub fn is_d_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_d_pin()
        }
        pub fn is_q_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_q_pin()
        }
        pub fn is_clk_pin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_clk_pin()
        }
        pub fn is_gate(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gate()
        }
        pub fn is_gate_in(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gate_in()
        }
        pub fn is_gate_out(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gate_out()
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_io()
        }
        pub fn set_walked(&self, walked: bool) {
            self.0.borrow().set_walked(walked)
        }
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, highlighted: bool) {
            self.0.borrow().set_highlighted(highlighted)
        }
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.0.borrow().get_gid()
        }
        pub fn is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_origin()
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedPhysicalPin) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().distance(other)
        }
        pub fn qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().qpin_delay()
        }
        pub fn record_origin_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().record_origin_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn change_origin_pin(&self, pin: WeakPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().change_origin_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn get_origin_pin(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().get_origin_pin()
        }
        pub fn ff_origin_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().ff_origin_pin()
        }
        pub fn previous_pin(&self) -> WeakPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().previous_pin()
        }
        pub fn get_origin_id(&self) -> usize {
            self.0.borrow().get_origin_id()
        }
        pub fn record_mapped_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().record_mapped_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn get_mapped_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().get_mapped_pin()
        }
        pub fn get_origin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow_mut().get_origin_delay()
        }
        pub fn set_origin_delay(&self, value: float) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().set_origin_delay(value)
        }
        pub fn get_slack(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow_mut().get_slack()
        }
        pub fn set_slack(&self, value: float) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().set_slack(value)
        }
        pub fn get_qpin_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().get_qpin_delay()
        }
        pub fn corresponding_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().corresponding_pin()
        }
    }
    impl WeakPhysicalPin {

    }
    impl fmt::Debug for PhysicalPin {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("PhysicalPin").field("name", &self.full_name()).finish()
        }
    }
    static PIN_NAME_MAPPER: LazyLock<Dict<&'static str, String>> = LazyLock::new(|| {
        Dict::from_iter([
            ("D", "Q".to_string()),
            ("Q", "D".to_string()),
            ("D0", "Q0".to_string()),
            ("Q0", "D0".to_string()),
            ("D1", "Q1".to_string()),
            ("Q1", "D1".to_string()),
            ("D2", "Q2".to_string()),
            ("Q2", "D2".to_string()),
            ("D3", "Q3".to_string()),
            ("Q3", "D3".to_string()),
        ])
    });
    pub struct Inst {
        pub name: String,
        pub x: float,
        pub y: float,
        pub lib: Reference<InstType>,
        pub libid: int,
        pub pins: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>,
        pub clk_neighbor: Reference<Vec<String>>,
        pub is_origin: bool,
        #[hash]
        pub gid: usize,
        pub walked: bool,
        pub highlighted: bool,
        pub origin_inst: Vec<WeakInst>,
        pub legalized: bool,
        pub optimized_pos: Vector2,
        pub locked: bool,
        /// Indicate that the inst is only partially connected to the netlist
        pub is_orphan: bool,
        pub clk_net: WeakNet,
        pub start_pos: OnceCell<Vector2>,
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for Inst {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            true && self.gid == other.gid
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for Inst {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for Inst {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            self.gid.hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct SharedInst(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>);
    impl SharedInst {
        pub fn new(value: Inst) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Inst> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Inst> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakInst {
            WeakInst(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        pub fn get_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.name)
        }
        pub fn get_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.name)
        }
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_x(&self) -> float {
            self.borrow().x
        }
        pub fn get_x_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<float> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.x)
        }
        pub fn set_x(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().x = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_y(&self) -> float {
            self.borrow().y
        }
        pub fn get_y_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<float> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.y)
        }
        pub fn set_y(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().y = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_lib(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Reference<InstType>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.lib)
        }
        pub fn get_lib_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Reference<InstType>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.lib)
        }
        pub fn set_lib(&self, value: Reference<InstType>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().lib = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_libid(&self) -> int {
            self.borrow().libid
        }
        pub fn get_libid_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<int> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.libid)
        }
        pub fn set_libid(&self, value: int) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().libid = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_pins(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pins)
        }
        pub fn get_pins_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pins)
        }
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_clk_neighbor(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Reference<Vec<String>>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.clk_neighbor)
        }
        pub fn get_clk_neighbor_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Reference<Vec<String>>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.clk_neighbor)
        }
        pub fn set_clk_neighbor(&self, value: Reference<Vec<String>>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().clk_neighbor = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_origin
        }
        pub fn get_is_origin_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_origin)
        }
        pub fn set_is_origin(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_origin = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.borrow().gid
        }
        pub fn get_gid_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<usize> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.gid)
        }
        pub fn set_gid(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().gid = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_walked(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().walked
        }
        pub fn get_walked_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.walked)
        }
        pub fn set_walked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().walked = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_highlighted(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().highlighted
        }
        pub fn get_highlighted_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.highlighted)
        }
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().highlighted = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_origin_inst(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Vec<WeakInst>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.origin_inst)
        }
        pub fn get_origin_inst_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Vec<WeakInst>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.origin_inst)
        }
        pub fn set_origin_inst(&self, value: Vec<WeakInst>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().origin_inst = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_legalized(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().legalized
        }
        pub fn get_legalized_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.legalized)
        }
        pub fn set_legalized(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().legalized = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_optimized_pos(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Vector2> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.optimized_pos)
        }
        pub fn get_optimized_pos_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Vector2> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.optimized_pos)
        }
        pub fn set_optimized_pos(&self, value: Vector2) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().optimized_pos = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_locked(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().locked
        }
        pub fn get_locked_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.locked)
        }
        pub fn set_locked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().locked = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_orphan(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_orphan
        }
        pub fn get_is_orphan_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_orphan)
        }
        pub fn set_is_orphan(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_orphan = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_clk_net(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<WeakNet> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.clk_net)
        }
        pub fn get_clk_net_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<WeakNet> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.clk_net)
        }
        pub fn set_clk_net(&self, value: WeakNet) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().clk_net = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_start_pos(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<OnceCell<Vector2>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.start_pos)
        }
        pub fn get_start_pos_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<OnceCell<Vector2>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.start_pos)
        }
        pub fn set_start_pos(&self, value: OnceCell<Vector2>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().start_pos = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for SharedInst {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedInst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedInst").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>> for SharedInst {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<Inst> for SharedInst {
        fn from(inner: Inst) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedInst> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedInst) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::PartialEq for SharedInst {
        fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
            *self.0.borrow() == *other.0.borrow()
        }
    }
    impl std::cmp::Eq for SharedInst {}
    impl std::hash::Hash for SharedInst {
        fn hash<H: std::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
            (&*self.0 as *const _ as usize).hash(state);
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakInst(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>);
    impl WeakInst {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedInst> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedInst::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_x(&self) -> float {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().x
        }
        pub fn set_x(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().x = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_y(&self) -> float {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().y
        }
        pub fn set_y(&self, value: float) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().y = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_lib(&self, value: Reference<InstType>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().lib = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_libid(&self) -> int {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().libid
        }
        pub fn set_libid(&self, value: int) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().libid = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: Vec<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_clk_neighbor(&self, value: Reference<Vec<String>>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().clk_neighbor = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_origin(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_origin
        }
        pub fn set_is_origin(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_origin = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_gid(&self) -> usize {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().gid
        }
        pub fn set_gid(&self, value: usize) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().gid = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_walked(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().walked
        }
        pub fn set_walked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().walked = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_highlighted(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().highlighted
        }
        pub fn set_highlighted(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().highlighted = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_origin_inst(&self, value: Vec<WeakInst>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().origin_inst = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_legalized(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().legalized
        }
        pub fn set_legalized(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().legalized = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_optimized_pos(&self, value: Vector2) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().optimized_pos = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_locked(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().locked
        }
        pub fn set_locked(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().locked = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_orphan(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_orphan
        }
        pub fn set_is_orphan(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_orphan = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_clk_net(&self, value: WeakNet) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().clk_net = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_start_pos(&self, value: OnceCell<Vector2>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().start_pos = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakInst {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakInst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakInst").field("is_expired", &self.is_expired()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>> for WeakInst {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakInst> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Inst>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakInst) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl Inst {
        pub fn new(name: String, x: float, y: float, lib: &Reference<InstType>) -> Self {
            let clk_neighbor = build_ref(Vec::new());
            let lib = clone_ref(lib);
            Self {
                name,
                x,
                y,
                lib,
                libid: 0,
                pins: Default::default(),
                clk_neighbor,
                is_origin: false,
                gid: 0,
                walked: false,
                highlighted: false,
                origin_inst: Vec::new(),
                legalized: false,
                optimized_pos: (x, y),
                locked: false,
                is_orphan: false,
                clk_net: Weak::new().into(),
                start_pos: OnceCell::new(),
            }
        }
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_gt(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::Gate(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            match *self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::IOput(_) => true,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn is_o(&self) -> bool {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::IOput(x) => !x.is_input,
                _ => false,
            }
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
        pub fn pos_vec(&self) -> Vector2 {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
        pub fn move_to<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&mut self, x: T, y: U) {
            self.x = x.float();
            self.y = y.float();
        }
        pub fn move_to_pos<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&mut self, pos: (T, U)) {
            self.x = pos.0.float();
            self.y = pos.1.float();
        }
        pub fn move_relative<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&mut self, dx: T, dy: U) {
            self.x += dx.float();
            self.y += dy.float();
        }
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.pins.iter().filter(|pin| pin.is_d_pin()).cloned().collect()
        }
        pub fn qpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            if !self.is_ff() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_ff()")
            }
            self.pins.iter().filter(|pin| pin.is_q_pin()).cloned().collect()
        }
        pub fn corresponding_pin(&self, pin_name: &str) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .find(|x| *x.get_pin_name() == PIN_NAME_MAPPER[pin_name])
                .unwrap()
                .clone()
        }
        pub fn clkpin(&self) -> &SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.pins.iter().find(|pin| pin.is_clk_pin()).unwrap()
        }
        pub fn clk_net_name(&self) -> String {
            self.clk_net.upgrade().map(|net| net.get_name().clone()).unwrap_or_default()
        }
        pub fn inpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            if !self.is_gt() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_gt()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_gate_in())
                .map(|pin| pin.borrow().full_name())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn outpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            if !self.is_gt() {
                ::core::panicking::panic("assertion failed: self.is_gt()")
            }
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_gate_out())
                .map(|pin| pin.borrow().full_name())
                .collect()
        }
        pub fn center(&self) -> Vector2 {
            let cell = self.lib.borrow();
            (
                self.x + cell.property_ref().width / 2.0,
                self.y + cell.property_ref().height / 2.0,
            )
        }
        pub fn original_center(&self) -> Vector2 {
            cal_center_from_points(
                &self
                    .dpins()
                    .iter()
                    .map(|x| x.ff_origin_pin().inst().start_pos())
                    .collect_vec(),
            )
        }
        pub fn start_pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.start_pos
                .get()
                .expect(
                    &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!("Start position not set for {0}", self.name),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                )
                .clone()
        }
        pub fn bits(&self) -> uint {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(inst) => inst.bits,
                _ => {
                    #[cold]
                    #[track_caller]
                    #[inline(never)]
                    #[rustc_const_panic_str]
                    #[rustc_do_not_const_check]
                    const fn panic_cold_display<T: ::core::fmt::Display>(arg: &T) -> ! {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_display(arg)
                    }
                    panic_cold_display(
                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!("{0} is not a flip-flop", self.name),
                                );
                                res
                            })
                            .red(),
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn power(&self) -> float {
            match &*self.lib.borrow() {
                InstType::FlipFlop(inst) => inst.power,
                _ => {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(format_args!("Not a flip-flop"));
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn width(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().width
        }
        pub fn height(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().height
        }
        pub fn area(&self) -> float {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().area
        }
        pub fn bbox(&self) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            let (x, y) = self.pos();
            let (w, h) = (self.width(), self.height());
            let buffer = 0.1;
            [[x + buffer, y + buffer], [x + w - buffer, y + h - buffer]]
        }
        pub fn position_bbox(&self) -> [float; 2] {
            let (x, y) = self.pos();
            [x, y]
        }
        pub fn lib_name(&self) -> String {
            self.lib.borrow_mut().property().name.clone()
        }
        pub fn assign_lib(&mut self, lib: Reference<InstType>) {
            self.lib = lib;
        }
        pub fn get_source_origin_insts(&self) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            let mut group = Vec::new();
            if self.is_origin {
                group.push(self.origin_inst[0].upgrade().unwrap());
            } else {
                group
                    .extend(
                        self.origin_inst.iter().flat_map(|x| x.get_source_origin_insts()),
                    );
            }
            group
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedInst) -> float {
            norm1(self.pos(), other.pos())
        }
        pub fn get_mapped_inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .next()
                .map_or_else(
                    || {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!("No pins found for inst {0}", self.name),
                        );
                    },
                    |pin| pin.borrow().get_mapped_pin().inst(),
                )
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&mut self, pin: PhysicalPin) {
            let pin: SharedPhysicalPin = pin.into();
            pin.record_mapped_pin(&pin);
            self.pins.push(pin);
        }
        pub fn set_corresponding_pins(&self) {
            for pin in self.pins.iter().filter(|x| x.is_d_pin() || x.is_q_pin()) {
                let corresponding_pin = self.corresponding_pin(&pin.get_pin_name());
                pin.set_corresponding_pin(Some(corresponding_pin));
            }
        }
    }
    impl SharedInst {
        pub fn is_ff(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_ff()
        }
        pub fn is_gt(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_gt()
        }
        pub fn is_io(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_io()
        }
        pub fn is_o(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.borrow().is_o()
        }
        pub fn pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().pos()
        }
        pub fn pos_vec(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().pos_vec()
        }
        pub fn move_to<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&self, x: T, y: U) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_to(x, y)
        }
        pub fn move_to_pos<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&self, pos: (T, U)) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_to_pos(pos)
        }
        pub fn move_relative<T: CCfloat, U: CCfloat>(&self, dx: T, dy: U) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().move_relative(dx, dy)
        }
        pub fn dpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().dpins()
        }
        pub fn qpins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().qpins()
        }
        pub fn corresponding_pin(&self, pin_name: &str) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().corresponding_pin(pin_name)
        }
        pub fn clkpin(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.0.borrow(), |a| a.clkpin())
        }
        pub fn clk_net_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().clk_net_name()
        }
        pub fn inpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.0.borrow().inpins()
        }
        pub fn outpins(&self) -> Vec<String> {
            self.0.borrow().outpins()
        }
        pub fn center(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().center()
        }
        pub fn original_center(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().original_center()
        }
        pub fn start_pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            self.0.borrow().start_pos()
        }
        pub fn bits(&self) -> uint {
            self.0.borrow().bits()
        }
        pub fn power(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().power()
        }
        pub fn width(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().width()
        }
        pub fn height(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().height()
        }
        pub fn area(&self) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().area()
        }
        pub fn bbox(&self) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            self.0.borrow().bbox()
        }
        pub fn position_bbox(&self) -> [float; 2] {
            self.0.borrow().position_bbox()
        }
        pub fn lib_name(&self) -> String {
            self.0.borrow().lib_name()
        }
        pub fn assign_lib(&self, lib: Reference<InstType>) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().assign_lib(lib)
        }
        pub fn get_source_origin_insts(&self) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            self.0.borrow().get_source_origin_insts()
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: &SharedInst) -> float {
            self.0.borrow().distance(other)
        }
        pub fn get_mapped_inst(&self) -> SharedInst {
            self.0.borrow().get_mapped_inst()
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&self, pin: PhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().add_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn set_corresponding_pins(&self) {
            self.0.borrow().set_corresponding_pins()
        }
    }

    impl fmt::Debug for Inst {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            let lib_name = if self.is_io() {
                "IOput".to_string()
            } else {
                self.lib.borrow().property_ref().name.clone()
            };
            f.debug_struct("Inst")
                .field("name", &self.name)
                .field("lib", &lib_name)
                .field("current_pos", &(self.x, self.y))
                .field("gid", &self.gid)
                .finish()
        }
    }

        pub num_cols: int,
