    impl PlacementRows {
        pub fn get_position(&self, column: i32) -> Vector2 {
            let x = self.x + column as float * self.width;
            let y = self.y;
            (x, y)
        }
    }
    pub struct Net {
        pub name: String,
        pub num_pins: uint,
        pub pins: LinkedHashSet<SharedPhysicalPin>,
        pub is_clk: bool,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Net {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "Net",
                "name",
                &self.name,
                "num_pins",
                &self.num_pins,
                "pins",
                &self.pins,
                "is_clk",
                &&self.is_clk,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for Net {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Net {
            Net {
                name: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                pins: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                is_clk: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    pub struct SharedNet(pub std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>);
    impl SharedNet {
        pub fn new(value: Net) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(value)))
        }
        pub fn borrow(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<Net> {
            self.0.borrow()
        }
        pub fn borrow_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<Net> {
            self.0.borrow_mut()
        }
        pub fn get_ref(&self) -> &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
            &self.0
        }
        pub fn downgrade(&self) -> WeakNet {
            WeakNet(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(&self.0))
        }
        pub fn get_name(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<String> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.name)
        }
        pub fn get_name_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<String> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.name)
        }
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_num_pins(&self) -> uint {
            self.borrow().num_pins
        }
        pub fn get_num_pins_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<uint> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.num_pins)
        }
        pub fn set_num_pins(&self, value: uint) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().num_pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_pins(&self) -> std::cell::Ref<LinkedHashSet<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::Ref::map(self.borrow(), |inner| &inner.pins)
        }
        pub fn get_pins_mut(
            &self,
        ) -> std::cell::RefMut<LinkedHashSet<SharedPhysicalPin>> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.pins)
        }
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: LinkedHashSet<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_clk(&self) -> bool {
            self.borrow().is_clk
        }
        pub fn get_is_clk_mut(&self) -> std::cell::RefMut<bool> {
            std::cell::RefMut::map(self.borrow_mut(), |inner| &mut inner.is_clk)
        }
        pub fn set_is_clk(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.borrow_mut().is_clk = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for SharedNet {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for SharedNet {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("SharedNet").field("inner", &self.0.borrow()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>> for SharedNet {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<Net> for SharedNet {
        fn from(inner: Net) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::new(std::cell::RefCell::new(inner)))
        }
    }
    impl From<SharedNet> for std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
        fn from(wrapper: SharedNet) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    pub struct WeakNet(pub std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>);
    impl WeakNet {
        pub fn new(value: &std::rc::Rc<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(std::rc::Rc::downgrade(value))
        }
        pub fn upgrade(&self) -> Option<SharedNet> {
            self.0.upgrade().map(SharedNet::from)
        }
        pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.strong_count() == 0
        }
        pub fn set_name(&self, value: String) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().name = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_num_pins(&self) -> uint {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().num_pins
        }
        pub fn set_num_pins(&self, value: uint) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().num_pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn set_pins(&self, value: LinkedHashSet<SharedPhysicalPin>) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().pins = value;
            self
        }
        pub fn get_is_clk(&self) -> bool {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().is_clk
        }
        pub fn set_is_clk(&self, value: bool) -> &Self {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().is_clk = value;
            self
        }
    }
    impl Clone for WeakNet {
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self(self.0.clone())
        }
    }
    impl std::fmt::Debug for WeakNet {
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
            f.debug_struct("WeakNet").field("is_expired", &self.is_expired()).finish()
        }
    }
    impl From<std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>> for WeakNet {
        fn from(inner: std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>>) -> Self {
            Self(inner)
        }
    }
    impl From<WeakNet> for std::rc::Weak<std::cell::RefCell<Net>> {
        fn from(wrapper: WeakNet) -> Self {
            wrapper.0
        }
    }
    impl Net {
        pub fn new(name: String, num_pins: uint) -> Self {
            Self {
                name,
                num_pins,
                pins: Default::default(),
                is_clk: false,
            }
        }
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.pins
                .iter()
                .filter(|pin| pin.borrow().is_clk_pin())
                .cloned()
                .collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&mut self, pin: SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.pins.insert(pin);
        }
        pub fn remove_pin(&mut self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.pins.remove(pin);
        }
        pub fn source_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.pins.front().cloned().expect("No pins in net")
        }
    }
    impl SharedNet {
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.borrow().clock_pins()
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&self, pin: SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().add_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn remove_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.borrow_mut().remove_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn source_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.borrow().source_pin()
        }
    }
    impl WeakNet {
        pub fn clock_pins(&self) -> Vec<SharedPhysicalPin> {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().clock_pins()
        }
        pub fn add_pin(&self, pin: SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().add_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn remove_pin(&self, pin: &SharedPhysicalPin) {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow_mut().remove_pin(pin)
        }
        pub fn source_pin(&self) -> SharedPhysicalPin {
            self.0.upgrade().unwrap().borrow().source_pin()
        }
    }
    pub struct Setting {
        pub alpha: float,
        pub beta: float,
        pub gamma: float,
        pub lambda: float,
        pub die_size: DieSize,
        pub num_input: uint,
        pub num_output: uint,
        pub library: ListMap<String, InstType>,
        pub num_instances: uint,
        pub instances: ListMap<String, SharedInst>,
        pub num_nets: uint,
        pub nets: Vec<SharedNet>,
        pub bin_width: float,
        pub bin_height: float,
        pub bin_max_util: float,
        pub placement_rows: Vec<PlacementRows>,
        pub displacement_delay: float,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Setting {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            let names: &'static _ = &[
                "alpha",
                "beta",
                "gamma",
                "lambda",
                "die_size",
                "num_input",
                "num_output",
                "library",
                "num_instances",
                "instances",
                "num_nets",
                "nets",
                "bin_width",
                "bin_height",
                "bin_max_util",
                "placement_rows",
                "displacement_delay",
            ];
            let values: &[&dyn ::core::fmt::Debug] = &[
                &self.alpha,
                &self.beta,
                &self.gamma,
                &self.lambda,
                &self.die_size,
                &self.num_input,
                &self.num_output,
                &self.library,
                &self.num_instances,
                &self.instances,
                &self.num_nets,
                &self.nets,
                &self.bin_width,
                &self.bin_height,
                &self.bin_max_util,
                &self.placement_rows,
                &&self.displacement_delay,
            ];
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_fields_finish(
                f,
                "Setting",
                names,
                values,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for Setting {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Setting {
            Setting {
                alpha: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                beta: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                gamma: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                lambda: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                die_size: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_input: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_output: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                library: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_instances: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                instances: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                num_nets: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                nets: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_width: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_height: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                bin_max_util: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                placement_rows: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                displacement_delay: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Setting {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Setting {
            Setting {
                alpha: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.alpha),
                beta: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.beta),
                gamma: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.gamma),
                lambda: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.lambda),
                die_size: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.die_size),
                num_input: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.num_input),
                num_output: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.num_output),
                library: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.library),
                num_instances: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.num_instances),
                instances: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.instances),
                num_nets: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.num_nets),
                nets: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.nets),
                bin_width: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.bin_width),
                bin_height: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.bin_height),
                bin_max_util: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.bin_max_util),
                placement_rows: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.placement_rows),
                displacement_delay: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.displacement_delay),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Setting {
        pub fn new(input_path: &str) -> Self {
            let mut setting = Self::parse(std::fs::read_to_string(input_path).unwrap());
            for inst in setting.instances.iter().map(|x| x.borrow()) {
                inst.get_start_pos().set((inst.get_x(), inst.get_y())).unwrap();
                inst.set_is_origin(true);
                inst.set_origin_inst(
                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([inst.downgrade()])),
                );
                for pin in inst.get_pins().iter() {
                    pin.record_origin_pin(pin);
                    pin.record_mapped_pin(pin);
                }
                inst.set_corresponding_pins();
            }
            setting
                .placement_rows
                .sort_by_key(|x| (OrderedFloat(x.x), OrderedFloat(x.y)));
            setting
        }
        pub fn parse(content: String) -> Setting {
            let mut setting = Setting::default();
            let mut instance_state = false;
            for raw in content.lines() {
                let line = raw.trim();
                if line.is_empty()
                    || match line.as_bytes().first() {
                        Some(b'#') => true,
                        _ => false,
                    }
                {
                    continue;
                }
                let mut it = line.split_whitespace();
                let key = it.next().unwrap();
                match key {
                    "Alpha" => {
                        setting.alpha = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "Beta" => {
                        setting.beta = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "Gamma" => {
                        setting.gamma = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "Lambda" => {
                        setting.lambda = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "DieSize" => {
                        let xl = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let yl = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let xu = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let yu = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        setting.die_size = DieSize::builder()
                            .x_lower_left(xl)
                            .y_lower_left(yl)
                            .x_upper_right(xu)
                            .y_upper_right(yu)
                            .build();
                    }
                    "NumInput" => {
                        setting.num_input = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "Input" | "Output" if !instance_state => {
                        let is_input = key == "Input";
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let x = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let y = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let ioput = InstType::IOput(IOput::new(is_input));
                        setting.library.push(name.to_owned(), ioput);
                        let lib_rc = setting.library.last().unwrap();
                        let inst = Inst::new(name.to_owned(), x, y, &lib_rc);
                        setting.instances.push(name.to_owned(), inst.into());
                        let inst_ref = setting.instances.last().unwrap();
                        {
                            let inst_borrow = inst_ref.borrow();
                            inst_borrow
                                .add_pin(
                                    PhysicalPin::new(
                                        &inst_borrow.clone(),
                                        &lib_rc.borrow().property_ref().pins[0],
                                    ),
                                );
                        }
                    }
                    "NumOutput" => {
                        setting.num_output = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "FlipFlop" => {
                        let bits = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let width = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let height = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let num_pins = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .library
                            .push(
                                name.to_owned(),
                                InstType::FlipFlop(
                                    FlipFlop::new(
                                        bits,
                                        name.to_owned(),
                                        width,
                                        height,
                                        num_pins,
                                    ),
                                ),
                            );
                    }
                    "Gate" => {
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let width = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let height = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let num_pins = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .library
                            .push(
                                name.to_owned(),
                                InstType::Gate(
                                    Gate::new(name.to_owned(), width, height, num_pins),
                                ),
                            );
                    }
                    "Pin" if !instance_state => {
                        let lib_rc = setting.library.last().unwrap();
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let x = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let y = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        lib_rc
                            .borrow_mut()
                            .property()
                            .pins
                            .push(name.to_owned(), Pin::new(name.to_owned(), x, y));
                    }
                    "NumInstances" => {
                        setting.num_instances = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                        instance_state = true;
                    }
                    "Inst" => {
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let lib_name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let x = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let y = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let lib = setting
                            .library
                            .get(&lib_name.to_string())
                            .expect("Library not found!");
                        setting
                            .instances
                            .push(
                                name.to_owned(),
                                Inst::new(name.to_owned(), x, y, lib).into(),
                            );
                        let last_inst = setting.instances.last().unwrap();
                        {
                            let lib_borrow = lib.borrow();
                            let inst_borrow = last_inst.borrow();
                            for lib_pin in lib_borrow.pins().iter() {
                                let physical_pin = PhysicalPin::new(
                                    &inst_borrow.clone(),
                                    lib_pin,
                                );
                                inst_borrow.add_pin(physical_pin);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    "NumNets" => {
                        setting.num_nets = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "Net" => {
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let num_pins = parse_next::<uint>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .nets
                            .push(SharedNet::new(Net::new(name.to_owned(), num_pins)));
                    }
                    "Pin" => {
                        let pin_token = next_str(&mut it);
                        let mut parts = pin_token.split('/');
                        let net_rc = setting.nets.last_mut().unwrap();
                        match (parts.next(), parts.next()) {
                            (Some(inst_name), None) => {
                                let pin = setting
                                    .instances
                                    .get(&inst_name.to_string())
                                    .unwrap()
                                    .borrow()
                                    .get_pins()[0]
                                    .clone();
                                pin.set_net_name(net_rc.get_name().clone());
                                net_rc.add_pin(pin);
                            }
                            (Some(inst_name), Some(pin_name)) => {
                                let inst = setting
                                    .instances
                                    .get(&inst_name.to_string())
                                    .expect("instance not found");
                                let pin = inst
                                    .borrow()
                                    .get_pins()
                                    .iter()
                                    .find(|p| *p.get_pin_name() == pin_name)
                                    .unwrap()
                                    .clone();
                                pin.set_net_name(net_rc.borrow().name.clone());
                                if pin.is_clk_pin() {
                                    net_rc.set_is_clk(true);
                                    if !inst.borrow().get_clk_net().upgrade().is_none() {
                                        ::core::panicking::panic(
                                            "assertion failed: inst.borrow().get_clk_net().upgrade().is_none()",
                                        )
                                    }
                                    inst.borrow_mut().set_clk_net(net_rc.downgrade());
                                }
                                net_rc.add_pin(pin);
                            }
                            _ => {
                                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                    format_args!("Invalid pin name"),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    "BinWidth" => {
                        setting.bin_width = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "BinHeight" => {
                        setting.bin_height = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "BinMaxUtil" => {
                        setting.bin_max_util = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "PlacementRows" => {
                        let x = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let y = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let width = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let height = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        let num_cols = parse_next::<int>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .placement_rows
                            .push(PlacementRows {
                                x,
                                y,
                                width,
                                height,
                                num_cols,
                            });
                    }
                    "DisplacementDelay" => {
                        setting.displacement_delay = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                    }
                    "QpinDelay" => {
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let delay = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .library
                            .get(&name.to_string())
                            .expect("QpinDelay: lib not found")
                            .borrow_mut()
                            .ff()
                            .qpin_delay = delay;
                    }
                    "TimingSlack" => {
                        let inst_name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let pin_name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let slack = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .instances
                            .get(&inst_name.to_string())
                            .expect("TimingSlack: inst not found")
                            .borrow()
                            .get_pins()
                            .iter()
                            .find(|x| *x.get_pin_name() == pin_name)
                            .unwrap()
                            .set_slack(slack);
                    }
                    "GatePower" => {
                        let name = next_str(&mut it);
                        let power = parse_next::<float>(&mut it);
                        setting
                            .library
                            .get(&name.to_string())
                            .expect("GatePower: lib not found")
                            .borrow_mut()
                            .ff()
                            .power = power;
                    }
                    _ => {}
                }
            }
            {
                {
                    match (
                        &(setting.num_input.usize() + setting.num_output.usize()),
                        &(setting
                            .instances
                            .iter()
                            .filter(|x| x.borrow().is_io())
                            .count()),
                    ) {
                        (left_val, right_val) => {
                            if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                            ": ",
                                            format_args!("{0}", "Input/Output count is not correct"),
                                            (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            };
            {
                {
                    match (
                        &(setting.num_instances.usize()),
                        &(setting.instances.len() - setting.num_input.usize()
                            - setting.num_output.usize()),
                    ) {
                        (left_val, right_val) => {
                            if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                {
                                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                        format_args!(
                                            "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                            ": ",
                                            format_args!(
                                                "{0}",
                                                ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                                            format_args!(
                                                                "Instances count is not correct: {0}/{1}",
                                                                setting.num_instances,
                                                                setting.instances.len() - setting.num_input.usize()
                                                                    - setting.num_output.usize(),
                                                            ),
                                                        );
                                                        res
                                                    })
                                                    .as_str(),
                                            ),
                                            (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                        ),
                                    );
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            };
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "NumInput: {0}, NumOutput: {1}, NumInstances: {2}, NumNets: {3}",
                                setting.num_input,
                                setting.num_output,
                                setting.num_instances,
                                setting.num_nets,
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::class",
                                "hello_world::class",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            if setting.num_nets != setting.nets.len().uint() {
                {
                    {
                        let lvl = ::log::Level::Warn;
                        if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                            ::log::__private_api::log(
                                { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                format_args!(
                                    "NumNets is wrong: ❌ {0} / ✅ {1}",
                                    setting.num_nets,
                                    setting.nets.len(),
                                ),
                                lvl,
                                &(
                                    "hello_world::class",
                                    "hello_world::class",
                                    ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                ),
                                (),
                            );
                        }
                    }
                };
                setting.num_nets = setting.nets.len().u64();
            }
            for net in &setting.nets {
                {
                    {
                        match (
                            &(net.get_pins().len()),
                            &(net.borrow().num_pins.usize()),
                        ) {
                            (left_val, right_val) => {
                                if !(*left_val == *right_val) {
                                    use ::pretty_assertions::private::CreateComparison;
                                    {
                                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                            format_args!(
                                                "assertion failed: `(left == right)`{0}{1}\n\n{2}\n",
                                                ": ",
                                                format_args!(
                                                    "Net \'{0}\' has {1} pins, but expected {2}",
                                                    net.get_name(),
                                                    net.get_pins().len(),
                                                    net.get_num_pins(),
                                                ),
                                                (left_val, right_val).create_comparison(),
                                            ),
                                        );
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    };
                };
            }
            setting
        }
    }
    pub struct PlacementInfo {
        pub bits: i32,
        pub positions: Vec<Vector2>,
    }
    impl PlacementInfo {
        ///Constructs a new `PlacementInfo`.
        pub fn new(bits: i32, positions: Vec<Vector2>) -> Self {
            PlacementInfo {
                bits: bits,
                positions: positions,
            }
        }
    }
    #[doc(hidden)]
    #[allow(
        non_upper_case_globals,
        unused_attributes,
        unused_qualifications,
        clippy::absolute_paths,
    )]
    const _: () = {
        #[allow(unused_extern_crates, clippy::useless_attribute)]
        extern crate serde as _serde;
        #[automatically_derived]
        impl _serde::Serialize for PlacementInfo {
            fn serialize<__S>(
                &self,
                __serializer: __S,
            ) -> _serde::__private::Result<__S::Ok, __S::Error>
            where
                __S: _serde::Serializer,
            {
                let mut __serde_state = _serde::Serializer::serialize_struct(
                    __serializer,
                    "PlacementInfo",
                    false as usize + 1 + 1,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::serialize_field(
                    &mut __serde_state,
                    "bits",
                    &self.bits,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::serialize_field(
                    &mut __serde_state,
                    "positions",
                    &self.positions,
                )?;
                _serde::ser::SerializeStruct::end(__serde_state)
            }
        }
    };
    #[doc(hidden)]

    impl PCell {
        pub fn get(&self, bits: i32) -> Vec<&PlacementInfo> {
            self.spatial_infos.iter().filter(|x| x.bits == bits).collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn filter(&mut self, rtree: &Rtree, (w, h): Vector2) {
            for placement_info in self.spatial_infos.iter_mut() {
                placement_info
                    .positions
                    .retain(|x| rtree.count([x.0, x.1], [w + x.0, h + x.1]) == 0);
            }
        }
    }

    pub struct PCellGroup<'a> {
        #[new(
            value = "geometry::Rect::from_coords([(f64::MAX,f64::MAX),(f64::MIN,f64::MIN)])"
        )]
        pub rect: geometry::Rect,
        #[new(default)]
        pub spatial_infos: Dict<i32, Vec<&'a Vec<Vector2>>>,
        #[new(default)]
        pub named_infos: Dict<String, Vec<&'a Vec<Vector2>>>,
        #[new(default)]
        pub range: ((usize, usize), (usize, usize)),
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<'a> ::core::fmt::Debug for PCellGroup<'a> {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "PCellGroup",
                "rect",
                &self.rect,
                "spatial_infos",
                &self.spatial_infos,
                "named_infos",
                &self.named_infos,
                "range",
                &&self.range,
            )
        }
    }
    impl<'a> PCellGroup<'a> {
        ///Constructs a new `PCellGroup`.
        pub fn new() -> Self {
            PCellGroup {
                rect: geometry::Rect::from_coords([
                    (f64::MAX, f64::MAX),
                    (f64::MIN, f64::MIN),
                ]),
                spatial_infos: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                named_infos: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                range: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    impl<'a> PCellGroup<'a> {
        pub fn add(&mut self, pcells: numpy::Array2D<&'a PCell>) {
            for pcell in pcells.iter() {
                for spatial_info in pcell.spatial_infos.iter() {
                    if spatial_info.positions.is_empty() {
                        continue;
                    }
                    self.spatial_infos
                        .entry(spatial_info.bits)
                        .or_insert(Vec::new())
                        .push(&spatial_info.positions);
                }
                self.rect.xmin = self.rect.xmin.min(pcell.rect.xmin);
                self.rect.xmax = self.rect.xmax.max(pcell.rect.xmax);
                self.rect.ymin = self.rect.ymin.min(pcell.rect.ymin);
                self.rect.ymax = self.rect.ymax.max(pcell.rect.ymax);
            }
        }
        pub fn add_pcell_array(&mut self, pcells: &'a PCellArray) {
            for pcell in pcells.elements.iter() {
                for (lib_idx, spatial_info) in pcell.spatial_infos.iter().enumerate() {
                    if spatial_info.positions.is_empty() {
                        continue;
                    }
                    self.spatial_infos
                        .entry(spatial_info.bits)
                        .or_insert(Vec::new())
                        .push(&spatial_info.positions);
                    self.named_infos
                        .entry(pcells.lib[lib_idx].name.clone())
                        .or_insert(Vec::new())
                        .push(&spatial_info.positions);
                }
                self.rect.xmin = self.rect.xmin.min(pcell.rect.xmin);
                self.rect.xmax = self.rect.xmax.max(pcell.rect.xmax);
                self.rect.ymin = self.rect.ymin.min(pcell.rect.ymin);
                self.rect.ymax = self.rect.ymax.max(pcell.rect.ymax);
            }
        }
        pub fn capacity(&self, bits: i32) -> usize {
            self.spatial_infos.get(&bits).map_or(0, |x| x.iter().map(|x| x.len()).sum())
        }
        pub fn get(&self, bits: i32) -> impl Iterator<Item = &Vector2> {
            self.spatial_infos[&bits].iter().flat_map(|x| x.iter())
        }
        pub fn get_all(&self) -> Vec<(i32, impl Iterator<Item = &Vector2>)> {
            self.spatial_infos.iter().map(|(&bit, _)| (bit, self.get(bit))).collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn center(&self) -> Vector2 {
            let (x, y) = self.rect.center();
            (x.float(), y.float())
        }
        pub fn distance(&self, other: Vector2) -> float {
            norm1(self.center(), other)
        }
        pub fn summarize(&self) -> Dict<i32, usize> {
            let mut summary = Dict::new();
            for (&bits, _) in self.spatial_infos.iter().sorted_by_key(|x| x.0) {
                summary.insert(bits, self.get(bits).count());
            }
            summary
        }
        pub fn iter(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = (i32, Vec<&Vector2>)> {
            self.spatial_infos.iter().map(|(k, _)| (*k, self.get(*k).collect()))
        }
        pub fn iter_named(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = (String, Vec<&Vector2>)> {
            self.named_infos
                .iter()
                .map(|(k, v)| (k.clone(), v.iter().flat_map(|x| x.iter()).collect()))
        }
    }
    pub struct LegalizeCell {
        pub index: usize,
        pub pos: Vector2,
        pub lib_index: usize,
        pub influence_factor: int,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for LegalizeCell {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field4_finish(
                f,
                "LegalizeCell",
                "index",
                &self.index,
                "pos",
                &self.pos,
                "lib_index",
                &self.lib_index,
                "influence_factor",
                &&self.influence_factor,
            )
        }
    }
    impl LegalizeCell {
        pub fn x(&self) -> float {
            self.pos.0
        }
        pub fn y(&self) -> float {
            self.pos.1
        }
    }

    pub struct CoverCell {
        pub x: float,
        pub y: float,
        pub is_covered: bool,
    }
    impl CoverCell {
        pub fn pos(&self) -> Vector2 {
            (self.x, self.y)
        }
    }
    pub struct UncoveredPlaceLocator {
        pub global_rtree: Rtree,
        available_position_collection: Dict<uint, (Vector2, Rtree)>,
        move_to_center: bool,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for UncoveredPlaceLocator {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> UncoveredPlaceLocator {
            UncoveredPlaceLocator {
                global_rtree: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                available_position_collection: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                move_to_center: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for UncoveredPlaceLocator {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> UncoveredPlaceLocator {
            UncoveredPlaceLocator {
                global_rtree: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.global_rtree),
                available_position_collection: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(
                    &self.available_position_collection,
                ),
                move_to_center: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.move_to_center),
            }
        }
    }
    impl UncoveredPlaceLocator {
        pub fn new(
            mbffg: &MBFFG,
            libs: &[Reference<InstType>],
            move_to_center: bool,
        ) -> Self {
            let gate_rtree = mbffg.generate_gate_map();
            let rows = mbffg.placement_rows();
            let die_size = mbffg.die_size();
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Debug;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "Die Size: ({0}, {1}), Placement Rows: {2}",
                                die_size.0,
                                die_size.1,
                                rows.len(),
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::class",
                                "hello_world::class",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            let available_position_collection = libs
                .iter()
                .map(|x| {
                    let binding = x.borrow();
                    let lib = &binding.ff_ref();
                    (lib.name().clone(), lib.bits(), lib.size())
                })
                .collect_vec()
                .into_par_iter()
                .map(|(name, bits, lib_size)| {
                    let positions = helper::evaluate_placement_resources_from_size(
                        &gate_rtree,
                        rows,
                        die_size,
                        lib_size,
                    );
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Debug;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!(
                                        "Bits: {0} [{1}], Size: {2:?}, Available Positions: {3}",
                                        bits,
                                        name,
                                        lib_size,
                                        positions.len(),
                                    ),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::class",
                                        "hello_world::class",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    let rtree = Rtree::from(
                        &positions
                            .iter()
                            .map(|&(x, y)| {
                                geometry::Rect::from_size(x, y, lib_size.0, lib_size.1)
                                    .bbox_p()
                            })
                            .collect_vec(),
                    );
                    (bits, (lib_size, rtree))
                })
                .collect();
            Self {
                global_rtree: mbffg.generate_gate_map(),
                available_position_collection,
                move_to_center,
            }
        }
        pub fn find_nearest_uncovered_place(
            &self,
            bits: uint,
            pos: Vector2,
        ) -> Option<Vector2> {
            if self.move_to_center {
                return Some(pos);
            }
            if let Some((lib_size, rtree)) = self
                .available_position_collection
                .get(&bits)
            {
                loop {
                    if rtree.size() == 0 {
                        return None;
                    }
                    let nearest_elements = rtree.get_all_nearest([pos.0, pos.1]);
                    let nearest_element = nearest_elements
                        .into_iter()
                        .min_by_key(|x| (
                            OrderedFloat(x.lower()[0]),
                            OrderedFloat(x.lower()[1]),
                        ))
                        .unwrap();
                    let nearest_pos = nearest_element.lower();
                    let bbox = geometry::Rect::from_size(
                            nearest_pos[0],
                            nearest_pos[1],
                            lib_size.0,
                            lib_size.1,
                        )
                        .bbox();
                    if self.global_rtree.count_bbox(bbox) == 0 {
                        return Some((nearest_pos).into());
                    } else {
                        {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                format_args!(
                                    "Position {0:?} is already covered by global rtree",
                                    nearest_pos,
                                ),
                            );
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!(
                        "No available positions for {0} bits: {1}",
                        bits,
                        self.available_position_collection.keys().join(", "),
                    ),
                );
            };
        }
        pub fn update_uncovered_place(&mut self, bits: uint, pos: Vector2) {
            if self.move_to_center {
                return;
            }
            let lib_size = &self.available_position_collection[&bits].0;
            let bbox = geometry::Rect::from_size(pos.0, pos.1, lib_size.0, lib_size.1)
                .bbox();
            if !(self.global_rtree.count_bbox(bbox) == 0) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("Position already covered"),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.global_rtree.insert_bbox(bbox);
            for (key, (_, rtree)) in &mut self.available_position_collection {
                let drains = rtree.drain_intersection_bbox(bbox);
            }
        }
        pub fn describe(&self) {
            let mut description = String::new();
            for (bits, (lib_size, rtree)) in &self.available_position_collection {
                description
                    .push_str(
                        &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!(
                                    "Bits: {0}, Size: ({1}, {2}), Available Positions: {3}",
                                    bits,
                                    lib_size.0,
                                    lib_size.1,
                                    rtree.size(),
                                ),
                            );
                            res
                        }),
                    );
            }
            description.print();
        }
        pub fn get(&self, bits: uint) -> Option<(Vector2, Vec<Vector2>)> {
            self.available_position_collection
                .get(&bits)
                .map(|x| (x.0, x.1.iter().map(|y| y.lower().into()).collect_vec()))
        }
    }
    pub struct Legalizor {
        pub uncovered_place_locator: UncoveredPlaceLocator,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Legalizor {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Legalizor {
            Legalizor {
                uncovered_place_locator: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(
                    &self.uncovered_place_locator,
                ),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Legalizor {
        pub fn new(mbffg: &MBFFG) -> Self {
            let uncovered_place_locator = UncoveredPlaceLocator::new(
                mbffg,
                &mbffg.find_all_best_library(),
                false,
            );
            Self { uncovered_place_locator }
        }
        pub fn legalize(&mut self, ff: &SharedInst) {
            let bits = ff.bits();
            let pos = ff.pos();
            let nearest_pos = self
                .uncovered_place_locator
                .find_nearest_uncovered_place(bits, pos)
                .expect("No available position found for legalization");
            ff.move_to(nearest_pos.0, nearest_pos.1);
            self.uncovered_place_locator.update_uncovered_place(bits, nearest_pos);
        }
    }
    pub struct VisualizeOption {
        #[builder(default = false)]
        pub shift_of_merged: bool,
        #[builder(default = false)]
        pub shift_from_origin: bool,
        #[builder(default = false)]
        pub shift_from_input: bool,
        #[builder(default = None)]
        pub bits: Option<Vec<usize>>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl VisualizeOption {
        /**
                Create a builder for building `VisualizeOption`.
                On the builder, call `.shift_of_merged(...)`(optional), `.shift_from_origin(...)`(optional), `.shift_from_input(...)`(optional), `.bits(...)`(optional) to set the values of the fields.
                Finally, call `.build()` to create the instance of `VisualizeOption`.
                */
        #[allow(dead_code, clippy::default_trait_access)]
        pub fn builder() -> VisualizeOptionBuilder<((), (), (), ())> {
            VisualizeOptionBuilder {
                fields: ((), (), (), ()),
                phantom: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[must_use]
    #[doc(hidden)]
    #[allow(dead_code, non_camel_case_types, non_snake_case)]
    pub struct VisualizeOptionBuilder<TypedBuilderFields = ((), (), (), ())> {
        fields: TypedBuilderFields,
        phantom: ::core::marker::PhantomData<()>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<TypedBuilderFields> Clone for VisualizeOptionBuilder<TypedBuilderFields>
    where
        TypedBuilderFields: Clone,
    {
        #[allow(clippy::default_trait_access)]
        fn clone(&self) -> Self {
            Self {
                fields: self.fields.clone(),
                phantom: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[allow(dead_code, non_camel_case_types, missing_docs)]
    #[automatically_derived]

                phantom: self.phantom,
            }
        }
    }

    #[automatically_derived]
    impl<
        __shift_of_merged: ::typed_builder::Optional<bool>,
        __shift_from_origin: ::typed_builder::Optional<bool>,
        __shift_from_input: ::typed_builder::Optional<bool>,
        __bits: ::typed_builder::Optional<Option<Vec<usize>>>,
    > VisualizeOptionBuilder<
        (__shift_of_merged, __shift_from_origin, __shift_from_input, __bits),
    > {
        #[allow(
            clippy::default_trait_access,
            clippy::used_underscore_binding,
            clippy::no_effect_underscore_binding
        )]
        pub fn build(self) -> VisualizeOption {
            let (shift_of_merged, shift_from_origin, shift_from_input, bits) = self
                .fields;
            let shift_of_merged = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(
                shift_of_merged,
                || false,
            );
            let shift_from_origin = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(
                shift_from_origin,
                || false,
            );
            let shift_from_input = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(
                shift_from_input,
                || false,
            );
            let bits = ::typed_builder::Optional::into_value(bits, || None);
            #[allow(deprecated)]
            VisualizeOption {
                shift_of_merged,
                shift_from_origin,
                shift_from_input,
                bits,
            }
                .into()
        }
    }

                                    );
                                }
                                _ => {
                                    let _ = _serde::de::MapAccess::next_value::<
                                        _serde::de::IgnoredAny,
                                    >(&mut __map)?;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        let __field0 = match __field0 {
                            _serde::__private::Some(__field0) => __field0,
                            _serde::__private::None => {
                                _serde::__private::de::missing_field("xmin")?
                            }
                        };
                        let __field1 = match __field1 {
                            _serde::__private::Some(__field1) => __field1,
                            _serde::__private::None => {
                                _serde::__private::de::missing_field("ymin")?
                            }
                        };
                        let __field2 = match __field2 {
                            _serde::__private::Some(__field2) => __field2,
                            _serde::__private::None => {
                                _serde::__private::de::missing_field("xmax")?
                            }
                        };
                        let __field3 = match __field3 {
                            _serde::__private::Some(__field3) => __field3,
                            _serde::__private::None => {
                                _serde::__private::de::missing_field("ymax")?
                            }
                        };
                        let __field4 = match __field4 {
                            _serde::__private::Some(__field4) => __field4,
                            _serde::__private::None => {
                                _serde::__private::de::missing_field("is_manhattan")?
                            }
                        };
                        _serde::__private::Ok(Rect {
                            xmin: __field0,
                            ymin: __field1,
                            xmax: __field2,
                            ymax: __field3,
                            is_manhattan: __field4,
                        })
                    }
                }
                #[doc(hidden)]
                const FIELDS: &'static [&'static str] = &[
                    "xmin",
                    "ymin",
                    "xmax",
                    "ymax",
                    "is_manhattan",
                ];
                _serde::Deserializer::deserialize_struct(
                    __deserializer,
                    "Rect",
                    FIELDS,
                    __Visitor {
                        marker: _serde::__private::PhantomData::<Rect>,
                        lifetime: _serde::__private::PhantomData,
                    },
                )
            }
        }
    };
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Rect {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_field5_finish(
                f,
                "Rect",
                "xmin",
                &self.xmin,
                "ymin",
                &self.ymin,
                "xmax",
                &self.xmax,
                "ymax",
                &self.ymax,
                "is_manhattan",
                &&self.is_manhattan,
            )
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::default::Default for Rect {
        #[inline]
        fn default() -> Rect {
            Rect {
                xmin: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                ymin: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                xmax: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                ymax: ::core::default::Default::default(),
                is_manhattan: ::core::default::Default::default(),
            }
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for Rect {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> Rect {
            Rect {
                xmin: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.xmin),
                ymin: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ymin),
                xmax: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.xmax),
                ymax: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ymax),
                is_manhattan: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.is_manhattan),
            }
        }
    }
    impl Rect {
        pub fn from_coords(coords: [(float, float); 2]) -> Self {
            Self {
                xmin: coords[0].0,
                ymin: coords[0].1,
                xmax: coords[1].0,
                ymax: coords[1].1,
                is_manhattan: false,
            }
        }
        pub fn coords(&self) -> (float, float, float, float) {
            (self.xmin, self.ymin, self.xmax, self.ymax)
        }
        pub fn from_center_and_size(
            middle: (float, float),
            width: float,
            height: float,
            is_manhattan: bool,
        ) -> Self {
            let half_width = width / 2.0;
            let half_height = height / 2.0;
            if !is_manhattan {
                Self {
                    xmin: middle.0 - half_width,
                    ymin: middle.1 - half_height,
                    xmax: middle.0 + half_width,
                    ymax: middle.1 + half_height,
                    is_manhattan,
                }
            } else {
                if !(width == height) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!(
                                "Width and height must be equal for Manhattan rectangles",
                            ),
                        );
                    }
                }
                Self {
                    xmin: middle.0,
                    ymin: middle.1 - half_width,
                    xmax: middle.0,
                    ymax: middle.1 + half_width,
                    is_manhattan,
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn from_size(xmin: float, ymin: float, width: float, height: float) -> Self {
            Self {
                xmin,
                ymin,
                xmax: xmin + width,
                ymax: ymin + height,
                is_manhattan: false,
            }
        }
        pub fn area(&self) -> float {
            (self.xmax - self.xmin) * (self.ymax - self.ymin)
        }
        pub fn center(&self) -> (float, float) {
            ((self.xmin + self.xmax) / 2.0, (self.ymin + self.ymax) / 2.0)
        }
        pub fn intersection(&self, other: &Rect) -> Option<Rect> {
            if !(!self.is_manhattan && !other.is_manhattan) {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!(
                            "Intersection is only defined for non-Manhattan rectangles",
                        ),
                    );
                }
            }
            let xmin = self.xmin.max(other.xmin);
            let ymin = self.ymin.max(other.ymin);
            let xmax = self.xmax.min(other.xmax);
            let ymax = self.ymax.min(other.ymax);
            if xmin < xmax && ymin < ymax {
                Some(Rect {
                    xmin,
                    ymin,
                    xmax,
                    ymax,
                    is_manhattan: false,
                })
            } else {
                None
            }
        }
        pub fn to_4_corners(&self) -> [(float, float); 4] {
            [
                (self.xmin, self.ymin),
                (self.xmin, self.ymax),
                (self.xmax, self.ymax),
                (self.xmax, self.ymin),
            ]
        }
        pub fn to_2_corners(&self) -> [(float, float); 2] {
            [(self.xmin, self.ymin), (self.xmax, self.ymax)]
        }
        pub fn wh(&self) -> (float, float) {
            (self.xmax - self.xmin, self.ymax - self.ymin)
        }
        /// Returns the bounding box of the rectangle with a small buffer
        pub fn bbox(&self) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            let buffer = 0.1;
            [
                [self.xmin + buffer, self.ymin + buffer],
                [self.xmax - buffer, self.ymax - buffer],
            ]
        }
        /// Returns the bounding box of the rectangle without a buffer
        pub fn bbox_p(&self) -> [[float; 2]; 2] {
            [[self.xmin, self.ymin], [self.xmax, self.ymax]]
        }
    }
    pub fn manhattan_square(middle: (float, float), half: float) -> [(float, float); 4] {
        [
            (middle.0, middle.1 - half),
            (middle.0 - half, middle.1),
            (middle.0, middle.1 + half),
            (middle.0 + half, middle.1),
        ]
    }
    pub fn rotate_point_45(x: float, y: float) -> (float, float) {
        (x + y, y - x)
    }
    pub fn rotate_point_inv_45(x: float, y: float) -> (float, float) {
        ((x - y) / 2.0, (x + y) / 2.0)
    }
    pub fn intersection_of_rects(rects: &Vec<Rect>) -> Option<Rect> {
        if rects.is_empty() {
            return None;
        }
        let mut intersection = rects[0].clone();
        for rect in &rects[1..] {
            match intersection.intersection(rect) {
                Some(new_intersection) => intersection = new_intersection,
                None => return None,
            }
        }
        Some(intersection)
    }
    pub fn joint_manhattan_square(
        rects: Vec<Rect>,
        rotate_back: bool,
    ) -> Option<[(f64, f64); 2]> {
        if !rects.iter().all(|r| r.is_manhattan) {
            {
                ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                    format_args!("All rectangles must be Manhattan squares"),
                );
            }
        }
        let cells: Vec<geometry::Rect> = rects
            .into_iter()
            .map(|rect| {
                geometry::Rect::from_coords([
                    rotate_point_45(rect.xmin, rect.ymin),
                    rotate_point_45(rect.xmax, rect.ymax),
                ])
            })
            .collect();
        match intersection_of_rects(&cells) {
            Some(x) => {
                let coord = x.to_2_corners();
                if rotate_back {
                    return coord
                        .iter()
                        .map(|x| geometry::rotate_point_inv_45(x.0, x.1))
                        .collect_vec()
                        .try_into()
                        .ok();
                }
                return Some(coord);
            }
            None => return None,
        }
    }
}

    pub struct Score {
        total_count: uint,
        io_count: uint,
        gate_count: uint,
        flip_flop_count: uint,
        alpha: float,
        beta: float,
        gamma: float,
        lambda: float,
        score: Dict<String, float>,
        weighted_score: Dict<String, float>,
        ratio: Dict<String, float>,
        bits: Dict<uint, uint>,
        lib: Dict<uint, Set<String>>,
        library_usage_count: Dict<String, int>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for Score {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            let names: &'static _ = &[
                "total_count",
                "io_count",
                "gate_count",
                "flip_flop_count",
                "alpha",
                "beta",
                "gamma",
                "lambda",
                "score",
                "weighted_score",
                "ratio",
                "bits",
                "lib",
                "library_usage_count",
            ];
            let values: &[&dyn ::core::fmt::Debug] = &[
                &self.total_count,
                &self.io_count,
                &self.gate_count,
                &self.flip_flop_count,
                &self.alpha,
                &self.beta,
                &self.gamma,
                &self.lambda,
                &self.score,
                &self.weighted_score,
                &self.ratio,
                &self.bits,
                &self.lib,
                &&self.library_usage_count,
            ];
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::debug_struct_fields_finish(f, "Score", names, values)
        }
    }

    type Vertex = SharedInst;
    type Edge = (SharedPhysicalPin, SharedPhysicalPin);
    pub trait IntoNodeIndex {
        fn node_index(self) -> NodeIndex;
    }
    impl IntoNodeIndex for usize {
        fn node_index(self) -> NodeIndex {
            NodeIndex::new(self)
        }
    }
    pub fn cal_center_from_points(points: &Vec<(float, float)>) -> (float, float) {
        let mut center = (0.0, 0.0);
        for &(x, y) in points.iter() {
            center.0 += x;
            center.1 += y;
        }
        center.0 /= points.len().float();
        center.1 /= points.len().float();
        center
    }
    pub fn cal_center(group: &[SharedInst]) -> (float, float) {
        if group.len() == 1 {
            return (group[0].get_x(), group[0].get_y());
        }
        let mut center = (0.0, 0.0);
        for inst in group.iter() {
            center.0 += inst.get_x();
            center.1 += inst.get_y();
        }
        center.0 /= group.len().float();
        center.1 /= group.len().float();
        center
    }
    pub fn cal_center_ref(group: &[&SharedInst]) -> (float, float) {
        if group.len() == 1 {
            return (group[0].get_x(), group[0].get_y());
        }
        let mut center = (0.0, 0.0);
        for inst in group.iter() {
            let k = inst.pos();
            center.0 += k.0;
            center.1 += k.1;
        }
        center.0 /= group.len().float();
        center.1 /= group.len().float();
        center
    }
    pub enum STAGE {
        Merging,
        TimingOptimization,
        DetailPlacement,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::marker::StructuralPartialEq for STAGE {}
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::cmp::PartialEq for STAGE {
        #[inline]
        fn eq(&self, other: &STAGE) -> bool {
            let __self_discr = ::core::intrinsics::discriminant_value(self);
            let __arg1_discr = ::core::intrinsics::discriminant_value(other);
            __self_discr == __arg1_discr
        }
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::fmt::Debug for STAGE {
        #[inline]
        fn fmt(&self, f: &mut ::core::fmt::Formatter) -> ::core::fmt::Result {
            ::core::fmt::Formatter::write_str(
                f,
                match self {
                    STAGE::Merging => "Merging",
                    STAGE::TimingOptimization => "TimingOptimization",
                    STAGE::DetailPlacement => "DetailPlacement",
                },
            )
        }
    }
    pub const fn stage_to_name(stage: STAGE) -> &'static str {
        match stage {
            STAGE::Merging => "stage_MERGING",
            STAGE::TimingOptimization => "stage_TIMING_OPTIMIZATION",
            STAGE::DetailPlacement => "stage_DETAIL_PLACEMENT",
        }
    }
    pub struct MBFFG {
        pub input_path: String,
        pub setting: Setting,
        pub graph: Graph<Vertex, Edge, Directed>,
        pass_through: Set<NodeIndex>,
        pareto_library: Vec<Reference<InstType>>,
        library_anchor: Dict<uint, usize>,
        current_insts: Dict<String, SharedInst>,
        disposed_insts: Vec<SharedInst>,
        pub prev_ffs_cache: Dict<SharedPhysicalPin, Set<PrevFFRecord>>,
        pub ffs_query: FFRecorder,
        /// orphan means no ff in the next stage
        pub orphan_gids: Vec<InstId>,
        pub debug_config: DebugConfig,
        pub filter_timing: bool,
        log_file: FileWriter,
        total_log_lines: Reference<uint>,
    }
    #[automatically_derived]
    impl ::core::clone::Clone for MBFFG {
        #[inline]
        fn clone(&self) -> MBFFG {
            MBFFG {
                input_path: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.input_path),
                setting: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.setting),
                graph: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.graph),
                pass_through: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.pass_through),
                pareto_library: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.pareto_library),
                library_anchor: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.library_anchor),
                current_insts: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.current_insts),
                disposed_insts: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.disposed_insts),
                prev_ffs_cache: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.prev_ffs_cache),
                ffs_query: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.ffs_query),
                orphan_gids: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.orphan_gids),
                debug_config: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.debug_config),
                filter_timing: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.filter_timing),
                log_file: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.log_file),
                total_log_lines: ::core::clone::Clone::clone(&self.total_log_lines),
            }
        }
    }
    impl MBFFG {
        pub fn new(input_path: &str) -> Self {
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!("Load file \'{0}\'", input_path),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            let setting = Setting::new(input_path);
            let graph = Self::build_graph(&setting);
            let mut mbffg = MBFFG {
                input_path: input_path.to_string(),
                setting: setting,
                graph: graph,
                pass_through: Set::new(),
                pareto_library: Vec::new(),
                library_anchor: Dict::new(),
                current_insts: Dict::new(),
                disposed_insts: Vec::new(),
                prev_ffs_cache: Dict::new(),
                ffs_query: Default::default(),
                orphan_gids: Vec::new(),
                debug_config: DebugConfig::builder().build(),
                filter_timing: true,
                log_file: FileWriter::new("tmp/mbffg.log"),
                total_log_lines: Reference::new(0.into()),
            };
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "Log file created at {0}",
                                mbffg.log_file.path(),
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            mbffg.pareto_front();
            mbffg.retrieve_ff_libraries();
            mbffg
                .current_insts
                .extend(
                    mbffg
                        .graph
                        .node_weights()
                        .filter(|x| x.is_ff())
                        .map(|x| (x.get_name().to_string(), x.clone().into())),
                );
            mbffg.create_prev_ff_cache();
            mbffg.report_lower_bound();
            mbffg
        }
        pub fn log(&self, msg: &str) {
            *self.total_log_lines.borrow_mut() += 1;
            let total_log_lines = *self.total_log_lines.borrow();
            if total_log_lines >= 1000 {
                if total_log_lines == 1000 {
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Warn;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!(
                                        "Log file has reached 1000 lines, skipping further logging.",
                                    ),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                }
                return;
            }
            self.log_file.write_line(msg).unwrap();
        }
        pub fn get_ffs_classified(&self) -> Dict<uint, Vec<SharedInst>> {
            let mut classified = Dict::new();
            for inst in self.get_all_ffs() {
                classified
                    .entry(inst.bits())
                    .or_insert_with(Vec::new)
                    .push(inst.clone());
            }
            classified
        }
        pub fn build_graph(setting: &Setting) -> Graph<Vertex, Edge> {
            let mut graph: Graph<Vertex, Edge> = Graph::new();
            for inst in setting.instances.iter() {
                let gid = graph.add_node(inst.borrow().clone()).index();
                inst.borrow().set_gid(gid);
            }
            for net in setting.nets.iter().filter(|net| !net.get_is_clk()) {
                let source = net.source_pin();
                let gid = source.get_gid();
                for sink in net.get_pins().iter().skip(1) {
                    graph
                        .add_edge(
                            NodeIndex::new(gid),
                            NodeIndex::new(sink.get_gid()),
                            (source.clone(), sink.clone()),
                        );
                }
            }
            graph
        }
        pub fn get_all_io(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.graph.node_weights().filter(|x| x.is_io())
        }
        pub fn get_all_gate(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.graph.node_weights().filter(|x| x.is_gt())
        }
        /// Returns an iterator over all flip-flops (FFs) in the graph.
        pub fn get_all_ffs(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.current_insts.values()
        }
        pub fn get_ffs_by_bit(&self, bit: uint) -> impl Iterator<Item = &SharedInst> {
            self.get_all_ffs().filter(move |x| x.bits() == bit)
        }
        pub fn get_ffs_sorted_by_timing(&self) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            self.current_insts
                .values()
                .map(|x| {
                    (
                        x.clone(),
                        Reverse(OrderedFloat(self.ffs_query.inst_effected_neg_slack(x))),
                    )
                })
                .sorted_by_key(|x| x.1)
                .map(|x| x.0)
                .collect_vec()
        }
        pub fn num_io(&self) -> uint {
            self.get_all_io().count().uint()
        }
        pub fn num_gate(&self) -> uint {
