                .iter()
                .map(|inst| {
                    let lib = self.get_lib(&inst.lib_name);
                    let new_ff = self.new_ff(&inst.name, &lib, false);
                    new_ff.move_to(inst.x, inst.y);
                    new_ff
                })
                .collect_vec();
            for (src_name, target_name) in mapping {
                let pin_from = self.get_pin_util(&src_name);
                let pin_to = self.get_pin_util(&target_name);
                self.transfer_edge(&pin_from, &pin_to);
            }
            for inst in ori_inst_names {
                self.remove_ff(&self.get_ff(&inst));
            }
            for inst in phy_insts {
                let ori_insts = inst
                    .dpins()
                    .iter()
                    .map(|x| x.get_origin_pin().inst())
                    .collect_vec();
                let new_ori_insts = ori_insts
                    .iter()
                    .unique_by(|x| x.get_gid())
                    .map(|x| x.downgrade())
                    .collect_vec();
                inst.get_origin_inst_mut().extend(new_ori_insts);
            }
        }
        pub fn remove_ff(&mut self, ff: &SharedInst) {
            if !ff.is_ff() {
                {
                    ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                        format_args!("{0} is not a flip-flop", ff.borrow().name),
                    );
                }
            }
            self.check_valid(ff);
            let gid = ff.get_gid();
            let node_count = self.graph.node_count();
            if gid != node_count - 1 {
                let last_indices = NodeIndex::new(node_count - 1);
                self.graph[last_indices].set_gid(gid);
            }
            self.graph.remove_node(NodeIndex::new(gid));
            self.current_insts.remove(&*ff.get_name());
            self.disposed_insts.push(ff.clone().into());
        }
        pub fn remove_inst(&mut self, gate: &SharedInst) {
            let gid = gate.get_gid();
            let node_count = self.graph.node_count();
            if gid != node_count - 1 {
                let last_indices = NodeIndex::new(node_count - 1);
                self.graph[last_indices].set_gid(gid);
            }
            self.graph.remove_node(NodeIndex::new(gid));
        }
        pub fn incomings_count(&self, ff: &SharedInst) -> usize {
            self.graph
                .edges_directed(NodeIndex::new(ff.get_gid()), Direction::Incoming)
                .count()
        }
        /// Splits all multi-bit flip-flops into single-bit flip-flops.
        pub fn debank_all_multibit_ffs(&mut self) -> Vec<SharedInst> {
            let mut count = 0;
            let mut debanked = Vec::new();
            for ff in self.get_all_ffs().cloned().collect_vec() {
                if ff.bits() > 1 {
                    let dff = self.debank(&ff);
                    debanked.extend(dff);
                    count += 1;
                }
            }
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!("Debanked {0} multi-bit flip-flops", count),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            debanked
        }
        pub fn displacement_delay(&self) -> float {
            self.setting.displacement_delay
        }
        pub fn timing_weight(&self) -> float {
            self.setting.alpha
        }
        pub fn power_weight(&self) -> float {
            self.setting.beta
        }
        pub fn area_weight(&self) -> float {
            self.setting.gamma
        }
        pub fn utilization_weight(&self) -> float {
            self.setting.lambda
        }
        fn update_inst_delay(&mut self, modified_inst: &SharedInst) {
            modified_inst
                .dpins()
                .iter()
                .for_each(|dpin| {
                    self.ffs_query.update_delay(&dpin.ff_origin_pin());
                });
        }
        pub fn update_delay_all(&mut self) {
            self.ffs_query.update_delay_all();
        }
        fn evaluate_utility(
            &mut self,
            instance_group: &[&SharedInst],
            uncovered_place_locator: &mut UncoveredPlaceLocator,
        ) -> float {
            let bit_width = instance_group.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).sum::<uint>();
            if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility {
                self.log(
                    &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "Evaluating utility for group of size {0}, bit width: {1}",
                                instance_group.len(),
                                bit_width,
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    }),
                );
            }
            let optimal_library = self.find_best_library_by_bit_count(bit_width);
            let ori_pos = instance_group.iter().map(|inst| inst.pos()).collect_vec();
            let utility = {
                let center = cal_center_ref(instance_group);
                let nearest_uncovered_pos = uncovered_place_locator
                    .find_nearest_uncovered_place(bit_width, center)
                    .unwrap();
                if self.debug_config.debug_nearest_pos {
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Debug;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!(
                                        "nearest uncovered pos: {0:?}, center: {1:?}, distance: {2}",
                                        nearest_uncovered_pos,
                                        center,
                                        norm1(nearest_uncovered_pos, center),
                                    ),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                }
                let ori_timing_score = self.group_eff_neg_slack(instance_group);
                let shift = instance_group
                    .iter()
                    .map(|x| norm1(x.pos(), nearest_uncovered_pos))
                    .collect_vec();
                instance_group
                    .iter()
                    .for_each(|inst| inst.move_to_pos(nearest_uncovered_pos));
                let new_pa_score = optimal_library
                    .borrow()
                    .ff_ref()
                    .evaluate_power_area_score(self);
                if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility
                    || self.debug_config.debug_banking_moving
                {
                    let new_timing_scores = instance_group
                        .iter()
                        .map(|x| self.inst_eff_neg_slack(x))
                        .collect_vec();
                    let message = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "PA score: {0}\nMoving \n{1}",
                                round(new_pa_score, 2),
                                instance_group
                                    .iter()
                                    .zip(new_timing_scores.iter())
                                    .zip(shift.iter())
                                    .map(|((x, &time_score), shift)| ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                            format_args!(
                                                "  {0}(sft: {1})(t_sc: {2})",
                                                x.get_name(),
                                                shift,
                                                round(time_score, 2),
                                            ),
                                        );
                                        res
                                    }))
                                    .join(",\n"),
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    });
                    self.log(&message);
                }
                let new_timing_score = self.group_eff_neg_slack(instance_group);
                if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility
                    || self.debug_config.debug_banking_moving
                {
                    let message = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "Timing change: {0} -> {1}\n-",
                                round(ori_timing_score, 2),
                                round(new_timing_score, 2),
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    });
                    self.log(&message);
                }
                let new_score = new_pa_score + new_timing_score * self.timing_weight();
                instance_group
                    .iter()
                    .zip(ori_pos)
                    .for_each(|(inst, pos)| {
                        inst.move_to_pos(pos);
                    });
                new_score
            };
            utility
        }
        fn partition_and_optimize_groups(
            &mut self,
            original_groups: &[Vec<SharedInst>],
            search_number: usize,
            max_group_size: usize,
            uncovered_place_locator: &mut UncoveredPlaceLocator,
        ) -> Vec<Vec<SharedInst>> {
            fn legalize(
                mbffg: &mut MBFFG,
                subgroup: &[&SharedInst],
                uncovered_place_locator: &mut UncoveredPlaceLocator,
            ) {
                let bit_width: uint = subgroup.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).sum();
                let optimized_position = cal_center_ref(&subgroup);
                let nearest_uncovered_pos = uncovered_place_locator
                    .find_nearest_uncovered_place(bit_width, optimized_position)
                    .unwrap();
                uncovered_place_locator
                    .update_uncovered_place(bit_width, nearest_uncovered_pos);
                for instance in subgroup.iter() {
                    instance.move_to_pos(nearest_uncovered_pos);
                    mbffg.update_inst_delay(instance);
                }
            }
            let mut final_groups = Vec::new();
            let mut previously_grouped_ids = Set::new();
            let instances = original_groups.iter().flat_map(|group| group).collect_vec();
            let rtree_entries = instances
                .iter()
                .map(|instance| (instance.position_bbox(), instance.get_gid()))
                .collect_vec();
            let mut rtree = RtreeWithData::new();
            rtree.bulk_insert(rtree_entries);
            let pbar = ProgressBar::new(instances.len().u64());
            pbar.set_style(
                ProgressStyle::with_template(
                        "{spinner:.green} [{elapsed_precise}] {bar:60.cyan/blue} {pos:>7}/{len:7} {msg}",
                    )
                    .unwrap()
                    .progress_chars("##-"),
            );
            for instance in instances.iter() {
                let instance_gid = instance.get_gid();
                if previously_grouped_ids.contains(&instance_gid) {
                    continue;
                }
                let mut candidate_group = ::alloc::vec::Vec::new();
                let mut start = true;
                while !rtree.is_empty() && candidate_group.len() < search_number {
                    let k: [float; 2] = instance.pos().into();
                    let rtree_nodes = rtree.get_all_nearest(k);
                    let rtree_node = if start {
                        rtree_nodes
                            .into_iter()
                            .find(|x| x.data == instance_gid)
                            .unwrap()
                            .clone()
                    } else {
                        rtree_nodes
                            .into_iter()
                            .sorted_by_key(|x| x.data)
                            .next()
                            .unwrap()
                            .clone()
                    };
                    rtree.delete_element(&rtree_node);
                    if start {
                        start = false;
                        continue;
                    }
                    let nearest_neighbor_gid = rtree_node.data;
                    if previously_grouped_ids.contains(&nearest_neighbor_gid) {
                        {
                            ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                                format_args!(
                                    "Found a previously grouped instance: {0}, but it should not be in the R-tree",
                                    nearest_neighbor_gid,
                                ),
                            );
                        };
                    }
                    let neighbor_instance = self.get_node(nearest_neighbor_gid).clone();
                    candidate_group.push(neighbor_instance);
                }
                if candidate_group.len() < search_number {
                    legalize(self, &[instance], uncovered_place_locator);
                    for g in candidate_group {
                        legalize(self, &[&g], uncovered_place_locator);
                    }
                    break;
                }
                let partition_combinations = if max_group_size == 4 {
                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([1])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([2])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([3])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0, 1])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([2, 3])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0, 2])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([1, 3])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0, 3])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([1, 2])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0, 1, 2, 3])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ]),
                    )
                } else if max_group_size == 2 {
                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0])),
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([1])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                    <[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([0, 1])),
                                ]),
                            ),
                        ]),
                    )
                } else {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!(
                                "Unsupported max group size: {0}",
                                max_group_size,
                            ),
                        );
                    };
                };
                if !(partition_combinations[0].len() == max_group_size) {
                    {
                        ::core::panicking::panic_fmt(
                            format_args!(
                                "Partition combinations should start with individual elements",
                            ),
                        );
                    }
                }
                let possibilities = candidate_group
                    .iter()
                    .combinations(max_group_size - 1)
                    .map(|combo| combo.into_iter().chain([*instance]).collect_vec())
                    .collect_vec();
                let mut combinations = Vec::new();
                for ((candidate_index, candidate_subgroup), (combo_idx, combo)) in ::itertools::Itertools::cartesian_product(
                    ::itertools::__std_iter::IntoIterator::into_iter(
                        possibilities.iter().enumerate(),
                    ),
                    ::itertools::__std_iter::IntoIterator::into_iter(
                        partition_combinations.iter().enumerate(),
                    ),
                ) {
                    if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility {
                        self.log(
                            &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!(
                                        "Try combination {0}/{1}: ",
                                        candidate_index,
                                        combo_idx,
                                    ),
                                );
                                res
                            }),
                        );
                    }
                    let mut utility = 0.0;
                    let mut valid_mask = Vec::new();
                    let mut partition_utilities = Vec::new();
                    for partition in combo {
                        let partition_ref = candidate_subgroup
                            .fancy_index_clone(partition);
                        let partition_utility = self
                            .evaluate_utility(&partition_ref, uncovered_place_locator);
                        valid_mask.push(true);
                        utility += partition_utility;
                        partition_utilities.push(round(partition_utility, 1));
                    }
                    combinations
                        .push((
                            utility,
                            candidate_index,
                            combo_idx,
                            partition_combinations[combo_idx]
                                .boolean_mask_ref(&valid_mask)
                                .into_iter()
                                .map(|x| candidate_subgroup.fancy_index_clone(x))
                                .collect_vec(),
                        ));
                    if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility {
                        let message = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!(
                                    "utility_sum = {0}, part_utils = {1:?}",
                                    round(utility, 2),
                                    partition_utilities,
                                ),
                            );
                            res
                        });
                        self.log(&message);
                        self.log(
                            "-----------------------------------------------------",
                        );
                    }
                }
                let (
                    best_utility,
                    best_candidate_index,
                    best_combo_index,
                    best_partition,
                ) = combinations.into_iter().min_by_key(|x| OrderedFloat(x.0)).unwrap();
                if self.debug_config.debug_banking_utility
                    || self.debug_config.debug_banking_best
                {
                    let message = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "Best combination index: {0}/{1}",
                                best_candidate_index,
                                best_combo_index,
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    });
                    self.log(&message);
                }
                for subgroup in best_partition.iter() {
                    legalize(self, subgroup, uncovered_place_locator);
                }
                let selected_instances = best_partition.iter().flatten().collect_vec();
                pbar.inc(selected_instances.len().u64());
                previously_grouped_ids
                    .extend(selected_instances.iter().map(|x| x.get_gid()));
                final_groups
                    .extend(
                        best_partition
                            .into_iter()
                            .map(|x| x.into_iter().cloned().collect_vec()),
                    );
                for instance in candidate_group
                    .iter()
                    .filter(|x| !previously_grouped_ids.contains(&x.get_gid()))
                {
                    let bbox = instance.position_bbox();
                    rtree.insert(bbox, instance.get_gid());
                }
            }
            pbar.finish_with_message("Merging completed");
            final_groups
        }
        pub fn merge(
            &mut self,
            physical_pin_group: &[SharedInst],
            max_group_size: usize,
            uncovered_place_locator: &mut UncoveredPlaceLocator,
        ) {
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "Merging {0} instances",
                                physical_pin_group.len(),
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            let instances = physical_pin_group
                .iter()
                .map(|x| {
                    (
                        x.clone(),
                        (
                            x
                                .dpins()
                                .iter()
                                .map(|x| {
                                    self.ffs_query.get_next_ffs_count(&x.ff_origin_pin())
                                })
                                .sum::<usize>(),
                            x.get_gid(),
                        ),
                    )
                })
                .sorted_by_key(|x| x.1)
                .collect_vec();
            let instances = instances.into_iter().map(|x| x.0).rev().collect_vec();
            const SEARCH_NUMBER: usize = 1;
            if !(SEARCH_NUMBER + 1 >= max_group_size) {
                ::core::panicking::panic(
                    "assertion failed: SEARCH_NUMBER + 1 >= max_group_size",
                )
            }
            let optimized_partitioned_clusters = self
                .partition_and_optimize_groups(
                    &[instances],
                    SEARCH_NUMBER,
                    max_group_size,
                    uncovered_place_locator,
                );
            let mut bits_occurrences: Dict<uint, uint> = Dict::new();
            for optimized_group in optimized_partitioned_clusters.into_iter() {
                let bit_width: uint = optimized_group.iter().map(|x| x.bits()).sum();
                *bits_occurrences.entry(bit_width).or_default() += 1;
                let pos = optimized_group[0].pos();
                let lib = &self.find_best_library_by_bit_count(bit_width);
                let new_ff = self.bank(optimized_group, lib);
                new_ff.move_to_pos(pos);
                new_ff.set_optimized_pos(pos);
            }
            bits_occurrences
                .iter()
                .for_each(|(bit_width, group_count)| {
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!(
                                        "Bit width: {0}, Total: {1}",
                                        bit_width,
                                        group_count,
                                    ),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                });
            self.update_delay_all();
        }
        pub fn replace_1_bit_ffs(&mut self) {
            let mut ctr = 0;
            for ff in self.get_all_ffs().filter(|x| x.bits() == 1).cloned().collect_vec()
            {
                let lib = self.find_best_library_by_bit_count(1);
                let ori_pos = ff.pos();
                let new_ff = self
                    .bank(<[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([ff])), &lib);
                new_ff.move_to_pos(ori_pos);
                ctr += 1;
            }
            self.ffs_query.update_delay_all();
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!(
                                "Replaced {0} 1-bit flip-flops with best library",
                                ctr,
                            ),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
            self.update_delay_all();
        }
        fn report_lower_bound(&self) {
            let pa = self
                .best_library()
                .borrow()
                .ff_ref()
                .evaluate_power_area_ratio(self);
            let total = self.num_bits().float() * pa;
            {
                {
                    let lvl = ::log::Level::Info;
                    if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL && lvl <= ::log::max_level() {
                        ::log::__private_api::log(
                            { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                            format_args!("Lower bound of score: {0}", total),
                            lvl,
                            &(
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                "hello_world::mbffg",
                                ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                            ),
                            (),
                        );
                    }
                }
            };
        }
        pub fn calculate_score(
            &self,
            timing: float,
            power: float,
            area: float,
        ) -> float {
            let timing_score = timing * self.timing_weight();
            let power_score = power * self.power_weight();
            let area_score = area * self.area_weight();
            timing_score + power_score + area_score
        }
        pub fn get_prev_ff_records(
            &self,
            dpin: &SharedPhysicalPin,
        ) -> &Set<PrevFFRecord> {
            self.prev_ffs_cache
                .get(&dpin.ff_origin_pin())
                .expect(
                    self
                        .error_message(
                            ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                                let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                    format_args!("No records for {0}", dpin.full_name()),
                                );
                                res
                            }),
                        )
                        .as_str(),
                )
        }
        pub fn move_ffs_to_center(&mut self) {
            for ff in self.get_all_ffs().collect_vec() {
                let center = cal_center(&ff.get_source_origin_insts());
                ff.move_to_pos(center);
            }
        }

Path: {file_name}\")\n    # P = PlotlyUtility(file_name, margin=0, showaxis=False)\n    # P.add_image(img)\n    # P.show(save=False)\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass VisualizeOptions:\n    pin_text: bool = True\n    pin_marker: bool = True\n    line: bool = True\n    cell_text: bool = True\n    io_text: bool = True\n    placement_row: bool = False\n\n\ndef visualize(\n    file_name, die_size, bin_width, bin_height, placement_rows, flip_flops, gates, io_pins, nets\n):\n    options = VisualizeOptions(\n        line=True,\n        cell_text=True,\n        io_text=True,\n        placement_row=False,\n    )\n\n    P = PlotlyUtility(file_name=file_name if file_name else \"output.html\", margin=30)\n    P.add_rectangle(\n        BoxContainer(\n            die_size.x_upper_right - die_size.x_lower_left,\n            die_size.y_upper_right - die_size.y_lower_left,\n            offset=(die_size.x_lower_left, die_size.y_lower_left),\n        ).box,\n        color_id=\"black\",\n        fill=False,\n        group=\"die\",\n    )\n\n    for i in range(0, math.ceil(die_size.x_upper_right / bin_width)):\n        for j in range(0, math.ceil(die_size.y_upper_right / bin_height)):\n            if i % 2 == 0:\n                if j % 2 == 1:\n                    continue\n            else:\n                if j % 2 == 0:\n                    continue\n            P.add_rectangle(\n                BoxContainer(\n                    bin_width,\n                    bin_height,\n                    offset=(i * bin_width, j * bin_height),\n                ).box,\n                color_id=\"rgba(44, line_width=1,\n    #             line_color=\"black\",\n    #             dash=False,\n    #         )\n    #         for i in range(row.num_cols):\n    #             P.add_line(\n    #                 (row.x + i * row.width, row.y),\n    #                 (row.x + i * row.width, row.y + row.height),\n    #                 group=\"row\",\n    #                 line_width=1,\n    #                 line_color=\"black\",\n    #                 dash=False,\n    #             )\n\n    #         # print(row)\n    #         # exit()\n    #         # for i in range(int(row.num_cols)):\n    #         #     P.add_line(\n    #         #         (row.x + i * row.width, row.y),\n    #         #         (row.x + i * row.width, row.y + row.height),\n    #         #         group=\"row\",\n    #         #         line_width=1,\n    #         #         line_color=\"black\",\n    #         #         dash=False,\n    #         #     )\n    #         # P.add_rectangle(\n    #         #     dash=True,\n    #         #     line_width=1,\n    #         # )\n    if len(flip_flops) + len(gates) <= 15:\n        options.pin_marker = True\n        options.pin_text = True\n    else:\n centers = km.cluster_centers_\n    cluster_sizes = np.bincount(labels)\n    if method == 0:\n        for cluster_id in range(max(labels) + 1):\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[np.where(cluster_sizes >= 4)] = np.inf\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 1:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                # print(\"--\")\n                # print(cluster_sizes[cluster_id])\n                # Find the farthest point from the cluster center\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = np.linalg.norm(points[cluster_points] - centers[cluster_id], axis=1)\n                farthest_point_idx = cluster_points[np.argmax(distances)]\n\n                # Reassign this point to the nearest other cluster\n                distances_to_centers = np.linalg.norm(points[farthest_point_idx] - centers, axis=1)\n                distances_to_centers[walked_id] = np.inf\n                # print(walked_id)\n                new_cluster_id = np.argmin(distances_to_centers)\n                # print(new_cluster_id)\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[farthest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    elif method == 2:\n        walked_id = []\n        while True:\n            cluster_id = next((i for i in range(K) if cluster_sizes[i] > 4), None)\n            if cluster_id is None:\n                break\n            walked_id.append(cluster_id)\n            while cluster_sizes[cluster_id] > 4:\n                cluster_points = np.where(labels == cluster_id)[0]\n                distances = scipy.spatial.distance.cdist(points[cluster_points], centers)\n                distances[:, walked_id] = np.inf\n                selected_idx, new_cluster_id = np.unravel_index(\n                    np.argmin(distances), distances.shape\n                )\n                cheapest_point_idx = cluster_points[selected_idx]\n\n                # Update labels and cluster sizes\n                labels[cheapest_point_idx] = new_cluster_id\n                cluster_sizes[cluster_id] -= 1\n                cluster_sizes[new_cluster_id] += 1\n    for i in range(len(km.cluster_centers_)):\n        km.cluster_centers_[i] = np.mean(points[np.where(labels == i)], axis=0)\n\n    return km\n\n\ndef evaluate(points, centers, labels, output=False):\n    km_obj = 0\n    for i, point in enumerate(points):\n        km_obj += np.linalg.norm(np.array(point) - np.array(centers[labels[i]]))\n    if output:\n        print(\"objective value:\", km_obj)\n    return km_obj\n\n\ndef plot_points_with_centers(points, centers, labels, colors):\n    plt.figure()\n lp_plot(points, N, method, labels):\n    M = np.abs(points).sum()\n    num_points = len(points)\n    K = num_points // N + 1  # Number of clusters\n    # colors = np.random.rand(K, 3)\n    index =       # model.Params.TimeLimit = 60\n            model.Params.WorkLimit = 120\n            model.Params.Threads = min(24, os.cpu_count())\n            # model.Params.ScaleFlag = 1\n            #             * x[i, j]\n                        )\n\n                model.setObjective(\n                    quicksum(\n                        quicksum((group_centroid_gap_abs[i, j]) for i in index) current_obj = model.cbGet(GRB.Callback.MIPSOL_OBJ)\n                    print(\"--------------------\")\n                    print(current_obj)\n                    # Check if it\'s the first solution or if improvement occurred\n                    if model._best_obj is None or current_obj < model._best_obj:\n                        model._best_obj = current_obj  # Update the best solution found\n print(\"grid_size:\", grid_size)\n    # print(\"tiles:\", tiles)\n    # print(\"tiles_weight:\", tiles_weight)\n    # print(\"tile_limits:\", tile_limits)\n    # print(\"spatial_occupancy:\", spatial_occupancy)\n    assert spatial_occupancy.shape == grid_size\n    # Define grid and tile sizes\n    N, M = grid_size  # Grid size (width, height)\n    # tiles = [(1, 2), (2, 1), (2, 2)]  # Tile types (width, height)\n    # tile_limits = [20, 25, 2]  # Limits for each tile type (max tiles)\n    # spatial_occupancy = np.transpose(spatial_occupancy)\n    # print(spatial_occupancy.shape)\n    tiles_area = [w * h for w, h in tiles]\n    # Create model\n    model = gp.Model(\"RectangularTiling\")\n    if not output:\n        model.Params.OutputFlag = 0\n    model.Params.Threads = min(24, os.cpu_count())\n    # Decision variables\n    x = model.addVars(len(tiles), N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"x\")  # Tile placement\n    y = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"y\")  # Cell coverage\n    y_weight = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS)\n\n    # Spatial occupancy constraints\n    # if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n    #     for i in range(N):\n    #         for j in range(M):\n    #             if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n    #                 for k in range(len(tiles)):\n    #                     model.addConstr(x[k, i, j] == 0)\n\n    # Tile placement constraints\n    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s within the bounds of any tile placement\n            model.addConstr(\n                y[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                )\n                + spatial_occupancy[i][j],\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n            model.addConstr(\n                y_weight[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c] / tiles_area[k] * tiles_weight[k]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                ),\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n\n    # Non-overlapping constraints: Each cell can be covered by at most one tile\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            model.addConstr(y[i, j] <= 1, name=f\"no_overlap_{i}_{j}\")\n\n    # Tile count limits\n    if len(tile_limits) > 0:\n        for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n            model.addConstr(\n                gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)) <= tile_limits[k],\n                name=f\"tile_limit_{k}\",\n            )\n\n    # Objective: Maximize total coverage\n    # model.setObjective(gp.quicksum(y[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE)\n    model.setObjective(\n        gp.quicksum(y_weight[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE\n    )\n\n    # Solve the model\n    model.optimize()\n    # Print solution\n    if model.status == GRB.OPTIMAL:\n        # print(\"Optimal solution found!\")\n        # for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        #     print(f\"Tile type {k} ({tile_h}x{tile_w}):\")\n        #     for i in range(N):\n        #         for j in range(M):\n        #             if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n        #                 print(f\"  Placed at ({i}, {j})\")\n\n        capcaity = np.zeros(len(tiles), dtype=int)\n        for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n            for i in range(N):\n                for j in range(M):\n                    if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                        capcaity[k] += 1\n        if output:\n            # draw layout using matplotlib\n            layout = np.zeros((N, M))\n            for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                            layout[i : i + tile_h, j : j + tile_w] = k + 1\n\n            if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n                            for k in range(len(tiles)):\n                                layout[i, j] = len(tiles) + 1\n            plot_binary_image(layout, aspect_ratio=1, title=\"Tile placements\", grid=True)\n            # layout = np.zeros((N, M))\n            # for i in range(N):\n            #     for j in range(M):\n            #         layout[i, j] = y_weight[i, j].x\n            # plot_binary_image(layout, aspect_ratio=1, title=\"Tile placements\", grid=True)\n            for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n                print(f\"Tile type {k} ({tile_h}x{tile_w}): {capcaity[k]}\")\n            print(\n                f\"Total coverage: {sum(capcaity[x]*tiles[x][0]*tiles[x][1] for x in range(len(capcaity)))/(grid_size[0] * grid_size[1])}\"\n            )\n\n        return capcaity\n    else:\n        print(\"No solution found.\")\n\n\ndef plot_pareto_curve(values, title=\"\", xlabel=\"\", ylabel=\"\"):\n    # Convert the data into a DataFrame and automatically generate item names\n    df = pd.DataFrame(\n        {\n            \"Item\": [f\"Item{i+1}\" for i in range(len(values))],  # Automatically generate item names\n            \"Value\": sorted(values, reverse=True),  # Decision variables\n    x = model.addVars(len(tiles), N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"x\")  # Tile placement\n    y = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"y\")  # Cell coverage\n    y_weight = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS)\n\n    # Spatial occupancy constraints\n    # if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n    #     for i in range(N):\n    #         for j in range(M):\n    #             if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n    #                 for k in range(len(tiles)):\n    #                     model.addConstr(x[k, i, j] == 0)\n\n    # Tile placement constraints\n    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    #         pub fn visualize_layout(
            &self,
            file_name: &str,
            visualize_option: VisualizeOption,
        ) {
            #[cfg(feature = "experimental")]
            {
                if !self.debug_config.debug_layout_visualization {
                    {
                        {
                            let lvl = ::log::Level::Warn;
                            if lvl <= ::log::STATIC_MAX_LEVEL
                                && lvl <= ::log::max_level()
                            {
                                ::log::__private_api::log(
                                    { ::log::__private_api::GlobalLogger },
                                    format_args!("Debug is disabled, skipping visualization"),
                                    lvl,
                                    &(
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        "hello_world::mbffg",
                                        ::log::__private_api::loc(),
                                    ),
                                    (),
                                );
                            }
                        }
                    };
                    return;
                }
                let file_name = {
                    let file = std::path::Path::new(&self.input_path);
                    ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                        let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                            format_args!(
                                "{0}_{1}",
                                file_name.to_string(),
                                &file.file_stem().unwrap().to_string_lossy().to_string(),
                            ),
                        );
                        res
                    })
                };
                let mut file_name = ::alloc::__export::must_use({
                    let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(format_args!("tmp/{0}", file_name));
                    res
                });
                let mut extra: Vec<PyExtraVisual> = Vec::new();
                if visualize_option.shift_from_origin {
                    file_name
                        += &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!("_shift_from_origin"),
                            );
                            res
                        });
                    extra
                        .extend(
                            self
                                .get_ffs_sorted_by_timing()
                                .iter()
                                .take(300)
                                .flat_map(|x| {
                                    x.dpins()
                                        .into_iter()
                                        .map(|pin| {
                                            PyExtraVisual::builder()
                                                .id("line")
                                                .points(
                                                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                                                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([
                                                            pin.ff_origin_pin().inst().start_pos(),
                                                            pin.inst().pos(),
                                                        ]),
                                                    ),
                                                )
                                                .line_width(5)
                                                .color((0, 0, 0))
                                                .arrow(false)
                                                .build()
                                        })
                                        .collect_vec()
                                })
                                .collect_vec(),
                        );
                }
                if visualize_option.shift_of_merged {
                    file_name
                        += &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!("_shift_of_merged"),
                            );
                            res
                        });
                    extra
                        .extend(
                            self
                                .get_all_ffs()
                                .map(|x| {
                                    let current_pos = x.pos();
                                    (
                                        x,
                                        Reverse(
                                            OrderedFloat(
                                                x
                                                    .get_source_origin_insts()
                                                    .iter()
                                                    .map(|origin| norm1(origin.start_pos(), current_pos))
                                                    .collect_vec()
                                                    .mean(),
                                            ),
                                        ),
                                    )
                                })
                                .sorted_by_key(|x| x.1)
                                .map(|x| x.0)
                                .take(1000)
                                .map(|x| {
                                    let mut c = x
                                        .get_source_origin_insts()
                                        .iter()
                                        .map(|inst| {
                                            PyExtraVisual::builder()
                                                .id("line".to_string())
                                                .points(
                                                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                                                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([inst.start_pos(), x.pos()]),
                                                    ),
                                                )
                                                .line_width(5)
                                                .color((0, 0, 0))
                                                .arrow(false)
                                                .build()
                                        })
                                        .collect_vec();
                                    c.push(
                                        PyExtraVisual::builder()
                                            .id("circle".to_string())
                                            .points(<[_]>::into_vec(::alloc::boxed::box_new([x.pos()])))
                                            .line_width(3)
                                            .color((255, 255, 0))
                                            .radius(10)
                                            .build(),
                                    );
                                    c
                                })
                                .flatten()
                                .collect_vec(),
                        );
                }
                if visualize_option.shift_from_input {
                    file_name
                        += &::alloc::__export::must_use({
                            let res = ::alloc::fmt::format(
                                format_args!("_shift_from_input"),
                            );
                            res
                        });
                    extra
                        .extend(
                            self
                                .get_ffs_sorted_by_timing()
                                .iter()
                                .take(10)
                                .flat_map(|x| {
                                    self.get_incoming_pins_for_instance(x)
                                        .into_iter()
                                        .map(|pin| {
                                            PyExtraVisual::builder()
                                                .id("line")
                                                .points(
                                                    <[_]>::into_vec(
                                                        ::alloc::boxed::box_new([pin.pos(), x.pos()]),
                                                    ),
                                                )
                                                .line_width(5)
                                                .color((0, 0, 0))
                                                .arrow(false)
                                                .build()
                                        })
                                        .chain(
                                            self
                                                .get_outgoing_pins_for_instance(x)
                                                .into_iter()
                                                .map(|pin| {
                                                    PyExtraVisual::builder()
                                                        .id("line")
                                                        .points(
                                                            <[_]>::into_vec(
                                                                ::alloc::boxed::box_new([pin.pos(), x.pos()]),
                                                            ),
                                                        )
                                                        .line_width(5)
                                                        .color((255, 0, 255))
                                                        .arrow(false)
                                                        .build()
                                                }),
                                        )
                                        .collect_vec()
                                })
                                .collect_vec(),
                        );
                }
                let file_name = file_name + ".png";
                if self.get_all_ffs().count() < 100 {
                    self.visualize_layout_helper(
                        false,
                        true,
                        extra,
                        &file_name,
                        visualize_option.bits,
                    );
                } else {
                    self.visualize_layout_helper(
                        false,
                        false,
                        extra,
                        &file_name,
                        visualize_option.bits,
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        pub fn die_size(&self) -> (float, float) {
            self.setting.die_size.top_right()
        }

Decision variables\n    x = model.addVars(len(tiles), N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"x\")  # Tile placement\n    y = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.BINARY, name=\"y\")  # Cell coverage\n    y_weight = model.addVars(N, M, vtype=GRB.CONTINUOUS)\n\n    # Spatial occupancy constraints\n    # if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n    #     for i in range(N):\n    #         for j in range(M):\n    #             if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n    #                 for k in range(len(tiles)):\n    #                     model.addConstr(x[k, i, j] == 0)\n\n    # Tile placement constraints\n    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        for i in range(N - tile_w + 1, N):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for j in range(M)) == 0)\n        for j in range(M - tile_h + 1, M):\n            model.addConstr(gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N)) == 0)\n\n    # Coverage constraints\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            # A cell (i, j) is covered if it\'s within the bounds of any tile placement\n            model.addConstr(\n                y[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                )\n                + spatial_occupancy[i][j],\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n            model.addConstr(\n                y_weight[i, j]\n                == gp.quicksum(\n                    x[k, r, c] / tiles_area[k] * tiles_weight[k]\n                    for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles)\n                    for r in range(max(0, i - tile_w + 1), i + 1)\n                    for c in range(max(0, j - tile_h + 1), j + 1)\n                    if r + tile_w <= N and c + tile_h <= M\n                ),\n                name=f\"cover_{i}_{j}\",\n            )\n\n    # Non-overlapping constraints: Each cell can be covered by at most one tile\n    for i in range(N):\n        for j in range(M):\n            model.addConstr(y[i, j] <= 1, name=f\"no_overlap_{i}_{j}\")\n\n    # Tile count limits\n    if len(tile_limits) > 0:\n        for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n            model.addConstr(\n                gp.quicksum(x[k, i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)) <= tile_limits[k],\n                name=f\"tile_limit_{k}\",\n            )\n\n    # Objective: Maximize total coverage\n    # model.setObjective(gp.quicksum(y[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE)\n    model.setObjective(\n        gp.quicksum(y_weight[i, j] for i in range(N) for j in range(M)), GRB.MAXIMIZE\n    )\n\n    # Solve the model\n    model.optimize()\n    # Print solution\n    if model.status == GRB.OPTIMAL:\n        # print(\"Optimal solution found!\")\n        # for k, (tile_w, tile_h) in enumerate(tiles):\n        #     print(f\"Tile type {k} ({tile_h}x{tile_w}):\")\n        #     for i in range(N):\n        #         for j in range(M):\n        #             if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n        #                 print(f\"  Placed at ({i}, {j})\")\n\n        capcaity = np.zeros(len(tiles), dtype=int)\n        for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n            for i in range(N):\n                for j in range(M):\n                    if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                        capcaity[k] += 1\n        if output:\n            # draw layout using matplotlib\n            layout = np.zeros((N, M))\n            for k, (tile_h, tile_w) in enumerate(tiles):\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if x[k, i, j].x > 0.5:\n                            layout[i : i + tile_h, j : j + tile_w] = k + 1\n\n            if len(spatial_occupancy) > 0:\n                for i in range(N):\n                    for j in range(M):\n                        if spatial_occupancy[i][j]:\n                            for k in range(len(tiles)):\n                                layout[i, j] = len(tiles) + 1\n            plot_binary_image(layout, aspect_ratio=1, title=\"Tile placements\", grid=True)\n            #
